Changelog
---------

### Tomcat 9.0.115 (remm)

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 3: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Prevent concurrent release of `OpenSSLEngine` resources and the termination of the Tomcat Native library as it can cause crashes during Tomcat shutdown. (markt) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 4: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add property "gpg.sign.files" to optionally disable release artefact signing with GPG. (rjung) 

### not released Tomcat 9.0.114 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 5: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69623](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69623): Additional fix for the long standing regression that meant that calls to `ClassLoader.getResource().getContent()` failed when made from within a web application with resource caching enabled if the target resource was packaged in a JAR file. (markt) 
*   ![Image 6: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Pull request [#923](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/923): Avoid adding multiple CSRF tokens to a URL in the `CsrfPreventionFilter`. (schultz) 
*   ![Image 7: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69918](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69918): Ensure request parameters are correctly parsed for HTTP/2 requests when the content-length header is not set. (dsoumis) 
*   ![Image 8: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update the minimum and recommended versions for Tomcat Native to 1.3.4. (markt) 
*   ![Image 9: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add a new `ssoReauthenticationMode` to the Tomcat provided Authenticators that provides a per Authenticator override of the SSO Valve `requireReauthentication` attribute. (markt) 
*   ![Image 10: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure URL encoding errors in the Rewrite Valve trigger an exception rather than silently using a replacement character. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 11: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid possible NPEs when using a TLS enabled custom connector. (remm) 
*   ![Image 12: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve warnings when setting ciphers lists in the FFM code, mirroring the tomcat-native changes. (remm) 
*   ![Image 13: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69910](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69910): Dereference TLS objects right after closing a socket to improve memory efficiency. (remm) 
*   ![Image 14: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Relax the JSSE vs OpenSSL configuration style checks on `SSLHostConfig` to reflect the existing implementation that allows one configuration style to be used for the trust attributes and a different style for all the other attributes. (markt) 
*   ![Image 15: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Better warning message when `OpenSSLConf` configuration elements are used with a JSSE TLS implementation. (markt) 
*   ![Image 16: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When using OpenSSL via FFM, don't log a warning about missing CA certificates unless CA certificates were configured and the configuration failed. (markt) 
*   ![Image 17: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) For configuration consistency between OpenSSL and JSSE TLS implementations, TLSv1.3 cipher suites included in the `ciphers` attribute of an `SSLHostConfig` are now always ignored (previously they would be ignored with OpenSSL implementations and used with JSSE implementations) and a warning is logged that the cipher suite has been ignored. (markt) 
*   ![Image 18: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add the `ciphersuite` attribute to `SSLHostConfig` to configure the TLSv1.3 cipher suites. (markt) 
*   ![Image 19: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add OCSP support to JSSE based TLS connectors and make the use of OCSP configurable per connector for both JSSE and OpenSSL based TLS implementations. Align the checks performed by OpenSSL with those performed by JSSE. (markt) 
*   ![Image 20: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for soft failure of OCSP checks with soft failure support disabled by default. (markt) 
*   ![Image 21: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for configuring the verification flags passed to `OCSP_basic_verify` when using an OpenSSL based TLS implementation. (markt) 
*   ![Image 22: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix OpenSSL FFM code compatibility with LibreSSL versions below 3.5. (remm) 
*   ![Image 23: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Prevent concurrent release of `OpenSSLEngine` resources and the termination of the Tomcat Native library as it can cause crashes during Tomcat shutdown. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 24: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69333](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69333): Correct a regression in the previous fix for [69333](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69333) and ensure that `reuse()` or `release()` is always called for a tag. (markt) 

#### Cluster

*   ![Image 25: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[62814](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=62814): Document that human-readable names maybe used for `mapSendOptions` and align documentation with `channelSendOptions`. Based on pull request [#929](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/929) by archan0621. (markt) 

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 26: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69920](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69920): When attempting to write to a closed `Writer` or `OutputStream` obtained from a WebSocket session, throw an `IOException` rather than an `IllegalStateExcpetion` as required by `Writer` and strongly suggested by `OutputStream`. (markt) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 27: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add `test.silent` property to suppress JUnit console output during test execution. Useful for cleaner console output when running tests with multiple threads. (csutherl) 
*   ![Image 28: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update the internal fork of Commons Pool to 2.13.1. (markt) 
*   ![Image 29: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update the internal fork of Commons DBCP to 2.14.0. (markt) 
*   ![Image 30: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update Commons Daemon to 1.5.1. (markt) 
*   ![Image 31: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update ByteBuddy to 1.18.3. (markt) 
*   ![Image 32: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update UnboundID to 7.0.4. (markt) 
*   ![Image 33: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update Checkstyle to 12.3.1. (markt) 
*   ![Image 34: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to French translations. (markt) 
*   ![Image 35: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Japanese translations provided by tak7iji. (markt) 
*   ![Image 36: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Chinese translations provided by Yang. vincent.h and yong hu. (markt) 
*   ![Image 37: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update Tomcat Native to 1.3.5. (markt) 

### 2025-12-07 Tomcat 9.0.113 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 38: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69871](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69871): Increase log level to INFO for missing configuration for the rewrite valve. (remm) 
*   ![Image 39: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add log warnings for additional Host `appBase` suspicious values. (remm) 
*   ![Image 40: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Remove hard dependency on tomcat-jni.jar for catalina.jar. `org.apache.catalina.Connector` no longer requires `org.apache.tomcat.jni.AprStatus` to be present. (markt) 
*   ![Image 41: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add the ability to use a custom function to generate the client identifier in the `CrawlerSessionManagerValve`. This is only available programmatically. Pull request [#902](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/902) by Brian Matzon. (markt) 
*   ![Image 42: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Change the SSO reauthentication behaviour for SPNEGO authentication so that a normal SPNEGO authentication is performed if the SSL Valve is configured with reauthentication enabled. This is so that the delegated credentials will be available to the web application. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 43: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Don't log an incorrect certificate `KeyStore` location when creating a TLS connector if the `KeyStore` instance has been set directly on the connector. (markt) 
*   ![Image 44: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) HTTP/0.9 only allows GET as the HTTP method. (remm) 
*   ![Image 45: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add `strictSni` attribute on the `Connector` to allow matching the `SSLHostConfig` configuration associated with the SNI host name to the `SSLHostConfig` configuration matched from the HTTP protocol host name. Non matching configurations will cause the request to be rejected. The attribute default value is `true`, enabling the matching. (remm) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 46: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69877](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69877): Catch IllegalArgumentException when processing URIs when creating the classpath to handle invalid URIs. (remm) 
*   ![Image 47: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix populating the classpath with the webapp classloader repositories. (remm) 

#### Clustering

*   ![Image 48: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct a regression introduced in 9.0.109 that broke some clustering configurations. (markt) 

#### Web Applications

*   ![Image 49: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Manager: Fix abrupt truncation of the HTML and JSON complete server status output if one or more of the web applications failed to start. (schultz) 
*   ![Image 50: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Manager: Include web application state in the HTML and JSON complete server status output. (markt) 
*   ![Image 51: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Documentation: Expand the documentation to better explain when OCSP is supported and when it is not. (markt) 

#### jdbc-pool

*   ![Image 52: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[64083](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=64083): If the underlying connection has been closed, don't add it to the pool when it is returned. Pull request [#235](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/235) by Alex Panchenko. (markt) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 53: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add test profile system for selective test execution. Profiles can be specified via `-Dtest.profile=<name>` to run specific test subsets without using patterns directly. Profile patterns are defined in `test-profiles.properties`. (csutherl) 
*   ![Image 54: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update file extension to media type mappings to align with the current list used by the Apache Web Server (httpd). (markt) 
*   ![Image 55: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update Commons Daemon to 1.5.0. (markt) 
*   ![Image 56: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update Byte Buddy to 1.18.2. (markt) 
*   ![Image 57: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update Checkstyle to 12.2.0. (markt) 
*   ![Image 58: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Spanish translations provided by White Vogel. (markt) 
*   ![Image 59: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to French translations. (remm) 
*   ![Image 60: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Japanese translations provided by tak7iji. (markt) 

### 2025-11-10 Tomcat 9.0.112 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 61: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When generating the class path in the Loader, re-order the check on individual class path components to avoid a potential `NullPointerException`. Identified by Coverity Scan. (markt) 
*   ![Image 62: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix SSL socket factory configuration in the JNDI realm. Based on pull request [#915](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/915) by Joshua Rogers. (remm) 
*   ![Image 63: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Add an attribute, `digestInRfc3112Order`, to `MessageDigestCredentialHandler` to control the order in which the credential and salt are digested. By default, the current, non-RFC 3112 compliant, order of salt then credential will be used. This default will change in Tomcat 12 to the RFC 3112 compliant order of credential then salt. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 64: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Graceful failure for OCSP on BoringSSL in the FFM code. (remm) 
*   ![Image 65: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69866](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69866): Fix a memory leak when using a trust store with the OpenSSL provider. Pull request [#912](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/912) by aogburn. (markt) 
*   ![Image 66: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix AJP message length check. Pull request [#916](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/916) by Joshua Rogers. (remm) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 67: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69862](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69862): Avoid NPE unwrapping Servlet exception which would hide some exception details. Patch submitted by Eric Blanquer. (remm) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 68: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update the internal fork of Apache Commons BCEL to 6.11.0. (markt) 
*   ![Image 69: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update to Byte Buddy 1.17.8. (markt) 
*   ![Image 70: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update to Checkstyle 12.1.1. (markt) 
*   ![Image 71: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update to Jacoco 0.8.14. (markt) 
*   ![Image 72: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update to SpotBugs 4.9.8. (markt) 
*   ![Image 73: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update to JSign 7.4. (markt) 
*   ![Image 74: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update Maven Resolver Ant Tasks to 1.6.0. (rjung) 
*   ![Image 75: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to French translations. (remm) 
*   ![Image 76: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Japanese translations provided by tak7iji. (markt) 

### 2025-10-13 Tomcat 9.0.111 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 77: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Log warnings when the SSO configuration does not comply with the documentation. (remm) 
*   ![Image 78: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Deprecate the `RemoteAddrFilter` and `RemoteAddrValve` in favour of the `RemoteCIDRFilter` and `RemoteCIDRValve`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 79: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69837](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69837): Fix corruption of the class path generated by the Loader when running on Windows. (markt) 
*   ![Image 80: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Reject requests that map to invalid Windows file names earlier. (markt) 
*   ![Image 81: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69839](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69839): Ensure that changes to session IDs (typically after authentication) are promulgated to the SSO Valve to ensure that SSO entries are fully clean-up on session expiration. Patch provided by Kim Johan Andersson. (markt) 
*   ![Image 82: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a race condition in the creation of the storage location for the `FileStore`. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 83: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69848](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69848): Fix copy/paste errors in 9.0.110 that meant DELETE requests received via the AJP connector were processed as OPTIONS requests and PROPFIND requests were processed as TRACE. (markt) 
*   ![Image 84: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Various OCSP processing issues in the OpenSSL FFM code. (dsoumis) 

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 85: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69845](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69845): When using `permessage-deflate` with Java 25 onwards, handle the underlying `Inflater` and/or `Deflater` throwing `IllegalStateException` when closed rather than `NullPointerException` as they do in Java 24 and earlier. (markt) 

### 2025-10-06 Tomcat 9.0.110 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 86: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Change the digest used to calculate strong ETags (if enabled) for the default Servlet from SHA-1 to SHA-256 to align with the recommendation in RFC 9110 that hash functions used to generate strong ETags should be collision resistant. (markt) 
*   ![Image 87: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct a regression in the fix for [69781](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69781) that broke `FileStore`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 88: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) HTTP methods are case-sensitive so always use case sensitive comparisons when comparing HTTP methods. (markt) 
*   ![Image 89: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69814](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69814): Ensure that `HttpSession.isNew()` returns `false` once the client has joined the session. (markt) 
*   ![Image 90: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Further performance improvements for ParameterMap. (jengebr/markt) 
*   ![Image 91: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a case-sensitivity issue in the trailer header allow list. (markt) 
*   ![Image 92: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Be proactive in cleaning up temporary files after a failed multi-part upload rather than waiting for GC to do it. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 93: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Add specific certificate selection code for TLS 1.3 supporting post quantum cryptography. Certificates defined with type `MLDSA` will be selected depending on the TLS client hello. (remm) 
*   ![Image 94: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Add `groups` attribute on `SSLHostConfig` allowing to restrict which groups can be enabled on the SSL engine. (remm) 
*   ![Image 95: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Optimize the conversion of HTTP method from byte form to String form. (markt) 
*   ![Image 96: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Store HTTP request headers using the original case for the header name rather than forcing it to lower case. (markt) 

#### Cluster

*   ![Image 97: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Prevent the channel configuration (sender, receiver, membership service) from being changed unless the channel is fully stopped. (markt) 

#### Web applications

*   ![Image 98: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Documentation. Clarify the purpose of the `maxPostSize` attribute of the `Connector` element. (markt) 
*   ![Image 99: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid NPE in manager webapp displaying certificate information. (remm) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 100: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update Byte Buddy to 1.17.7. (markt) 
*   ![Image 101: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update Checkstyle to 11.1.0. (markt) 
*   ![Image 102: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update SpotBugs to 4.9.6. (markt) 
*   ![Image 103: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update Jsign to 7.2. (markt) 
*   ![Image 104: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Russian translations provided by usmazat. (markt) 
*   ![Image 105: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to French translations. (remm) 
*   ![Image 106: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Japanese translations provided by tak7iji. (markt) 
*   ![Image 107: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Minor refactoring in JULI loggers. Patch provided by minjund. (schultz) 

### 2025-09-05 Tomcat 9.0.109 (remm)

Based on pull request [#882](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/882) by Aaron Ogburn. (markt) 
*   ![Image 110: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix handling of `QSA` and `QSD` flags in `RewriteValve`. (markt)

*   ![Image 112: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure keys are handed out to OpenSSL even if `PEMFile` fails to process it, with appropriate logging. (remm) 
*   ![Image 113: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add new `ML-DSA` key algorithm to `PEMFile` and improve reporting when reading a key fails. (remm) 
*   ![Image 114: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix possible early timeouts for network operations caused by a spurious wake-up of a waiting thread. Found by Coverity Scan. (markt)

*   ![Image 115: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Handle spurious wake-ups during leader election for `NonBlockingCoordinator`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 116: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Handle spurious wake-ups during sending of messages by `RpcChannel`. (markt) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 118: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add escaping to log formatters to align with JSON formatter. (markt) 
*   ![Image 119: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update Checkstyle to 11.0.0. (markt)

Pull request provided by Paulo Almeida. (markt) 
*   ![Image 157: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Provide finer grained control of multi-part request processing via two new attributes on the `Connector` element. `maxPartCount` limits the total number of parts in a multi-part request and `maxPartHeaderSize` limits the size of the headers provided with each part. Add support for these new attributes to the `ParameterLimitValve`. (markt)

### not released Tomcat 9.0.103 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 192: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Return 400 if the amount of content sent for a partial PUT is inconsistent with the range that was specified. (remm) 
*   ![Image 193: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add a new `RateLimiter` implementation, `org.apache.catalina.util.ExactRateLimiter`, that can be used with `org.apache.catalina.filters.RateLimitFilter` to provide rate limit based on the exact values configured. Based on pull request [#794](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/794) by Chenjp. (markt) 
*   ![Image 194: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix parsing of the `time-taken` token in the `ExtendedAccessLogValve`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 195: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix invocation of the FFM OpenSSL code for setting a SSL engine and FIPS mode. (remm) 
*   ![Image 196: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69600](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69600): Add IPv6 local addresses (RFC 4193 and RFC 4291) to the default internal proxies for the RemoteIpFilter and RemoteIpValve. (markt) 
*   ![Image 197: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69615](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69615): Improve integration with the not found class resources cache for users who are using a custom web application class loader and/or using reflection to dynamically add external repositories to the web application class loader. (markt) 
*   ![Image 198: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add a new initialisation parameter to the Default servlet - `allowPostAsGet` - which controls whether a direct request (i.e. not a forward or an include) for a static resource using the POST method will be processed as if the GET method had been used. If not allowed, the request will be rejected. The default behaviour of processing the request as if the GET method had been used is unchanged. (markt) 
*   ![Image 199: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69623](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69623): Correct a long standing regression that meant that calls to `ClassLoader.getResource().getContent()` failed when made from within a web application with resource caching enabled. (markt) 
*   ![Image 200: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69634](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69634): Avoid NPE on `JsonErrorReportValve`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 201: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add missing `throwable` stack trace to `JsonErrorReportValve` equivalent to the one from `ErrorReportValve`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 202: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve the handling of `%nn` URL encoding in the RewriteValve and document how `%nn` URL encoding may be used with rewrite rules. (markt) 
*   ![Image 203: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a potential exception when calling `WebappClassLoaderBase.getResource("")`. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 204: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69607](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69607): Allow failed initialization of MD5. Based on code submitted by Shivam Verma. (remm) 
*   ![Image 205: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69614](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69614): HTTP/2 priority frames with an invalid priority field value should be ignored. (markt) 
*   ![Image 206: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve handling of unexpected errors during HTTP/2 processing. (markt) 
*   ![Image 207: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add missing code to process an OpenSSL profile, such as `PROFILE=SYSTEM`, using FFM. (remm) 
*   ![Image 208: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Simplify the process of using a custom SSLContext for an HTTPS enabled connector. Based on pull request [#805](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/805) by Hakky54. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 209: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Replace custom URL encoding provided by the JSP runtime library with calls to `java.net.URLEncoder.encode()`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 210: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add compiler using the `Java Compiler` API, supporting exploded web applications. The `compilerClassName` to use is `org.apache.jasper.compiler.JavaCompiler`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 211: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for specifying Java 25 (with the value `25`) as the compiler source and/or compiler target for JSP compilation. If used with an Eclipse JDT compiler version that does not support these values, a warning will be logged and the default will be used. (markt) 

#### Cluster

### not released Tomcat 9.0.101 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 223: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When looking up class loader resources by resource name, the resource name should not start with '/'. If the resource name does start with '/', Tomcat is lenient and looks it up as if the '/' was not present. When the web application class loader was configured with external repositories and names starting with '/' were used for lookups, it was possible that cached 'not found' results could effectively hide lookup results using the correct resource name. (markt) 
*   ![Image 224: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Enable the JNDIRealm to validate credentials provided to `HttpServletRequest.login(String username, String password)` when the realm is configured to use GSSAPI authentication. (markt) 
*   ![Image 225: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a bug in the JRE compatibility detection that incorrectly identified Java 19 and Java 20 as supporting Java 21 features. (markt) 
*   ![Image 226: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve the checks for exposure to and protection against CVE-2024-56337 so that reflection is not used unless required. The checks for whether the file system is case sensitive or not have been removed. (markt) 
*   ![Image 227: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid scenarios where temporary files used for partial PUT would not be deleted. (remm) 
*   ![Image 228: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69602](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69602): Fix regression in releases from 12-2024 that were too strict and rejected weak etags in the `If-Range` header. (remm) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 229: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69575](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69575): Avoid using compression if a response is already compressed using `compress`, `deflate` or `zstd`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 230: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Use `Transfer-Encoding` for compression rather than `Content-Encoding` if the client submits a `TE` header containing `gzip`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 231: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a race condition in the handling of HTTP/2 stream reset that could cause unexpected 500 responses. (markt) 

#### Cluster

*   ![Image 232: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[69598](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69598): Add detection of service account token changes to the `KubernetesMembershipProvider` implementation and reload the token if it changes. Based on a patch by Miroslav Jezbera. (markt) 

#### Other

(markt)

*   ![Image 288: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add strong ETag support for the WebDAV and default servlet, which can be enabled by using the `useStrongETags` init parameter with a value set to `true`. The ETag generated will be a SHA-1 checksum of the resource content. (remm) 
*   ![Image 289: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Use client locale for directory listings. (remm) 
*   ![Image 290: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69439](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69439): Improve the handling of multiple `Cache-Control` headers in the `ExpiresFilter`. *   ![Image 291: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69447](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69447): Update the support for caching classes the web application class loader cannot find to take account of classes loaded from external repositories. Prior to this fix, these classes could be incorrectly marked as not found. (markt) 
*   ![Image 292: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69466](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69466): Rework handling of HEAD requests. Headers explicitly set by users will not be removed and any header present in a HEAD request will also be present in the equivalent GET request. There may be some headers, as per RFC 9110, section 9.3.2, that are present in a GET request that are not present in the equivalent HEAD request. (markt) 
*   ![Image 293: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69471](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69471): Log instances of `CloseNowException` caught by `ApplicationDispatcher.invoke()` at debug level rather than error level as they are very likely to have been caused by a client disconnection or similar I/O issue. (markt) 
*   ![Image 294: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add a test case for the fix for [69442](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69442). Also refactor references to `application/x-www-form-urlencoded`. Based on pull request [#779](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/779) by Chenjp. (markt) 
*   ![Image 295: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69476](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69476): Catch possible ISE when trying to report PUT failure in the `DefaultServlet`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 296: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for [RateLimit header fields for HTTP (draft)](https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/draft-ietf-httpapi-ratelimit-headers) in the `RateLimitFilter`. Based on pull request [#775](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/775) provided by Chenjp. (markt) 
*   ![Image 297: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[#787](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/787): Add regression tests for [69478](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69478). Pull request provided by Thomas Krisch. (markt) 
*   ![Image 298: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) The default servlet now rejects HTTP range requests when two or more of the requested ranges overlap. Based on pull request [#782](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/782) provided by Chenjp. (markt) 
*   ![Image 299: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Enhance Content-Range verification for partial PUT requests handled by the default servlet. Provided by Chenjp in pull request [#778](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/778). (markt) 
*   ![Image 300: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Harmonize `DataSourceStore` lookup in the global resources to optionally avoid the `comp/env` prefix which is usually not used there. (remm) 
*   ![Image 301: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) As required by RFC 9110, the HTTP `Range` header will now only be processed for `GET` requests. Based on pull request [#790](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/790) provided by Chenjp. (markt) 
*   ![Image 302: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Deprecate the `useAcceptRanges` initialisation parameter for the default servlet. It will be removed in Tomcat 12 onwards where it will effectively be hard coded to `true`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 303: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add `DataSource` based property storage for the `WebdavServlet`. (remm) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 304: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Align `encodedSolidusHandling` with the Servlet specification. If the pass-through mode is used, any `%25` sequences will now also be passed through to avoid errors and/or corruption when the application decodes the path. (markt) 

#### Jasper

### 2024-11-09 Tomcat 9.0.97 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 325: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for the new Servlet API method `HttpServletResponse.sendEarlyHints()`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 326: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)55470: Add debug logging that reports the class path when a `ClassNotFoundException` occurs in the digester or the web application class loader. Based on a patch by Ralf Hauser. (markt) 
*   ![Image 327: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif)[69374](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69374): Properly separate between table header and body in `DefaultServlet`'s listing. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 328: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif)[69373](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69373): Make `DefaultServlet`'s HTML listing file last modified rendering better (flexible). (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 329: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Improve HTML output of `DefaultServlet`. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 330: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor `RateLimitFilter` to use `FilterBase` as the base class. The primary advantage for doing this is less code to process `init-param` values. (markt) 
*   ![Image 331: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif)[69370](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69370): `DefaultServlet`'s HTML listing uses incorrect labels. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 332: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid NPE in `CrawlerSessionManagerValve` for partially mapped requests. (remm) 
*   ![Image 333: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add missing WebDAV `Lock-Token` header in the response when locking a folder. (remm) 
*   ![Image 334: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Invalid WebDAV lock requests should be rejected with 400. (remm) 
*   ![Image 335: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix regression in WebDAV when attempting to unlock a collection. (remm) 
*   ![Image 336: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Verify that destination is not locked for a WebDAV copy operation. (remm) 
*   ![Image 337: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Send 415 response to WebDAV `MKCOL` operations that include a request body since this is optional and unsupported. (remm) 
*   ![Image 338: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Enforce `DAV:` namespace on WebDAV XML elements. (remm) 
*   ![Image 339: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Do not allow a new WebDAV lock on a child resource if a parent collection is locked (RFC 4918 section 6.1). (remm) 
*   ![Image 340: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) WebDAV `DELETE` should remove any existing lock on successfully deleted resources. (remm) 
*   ![Image 341: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Remove WebDAV lock null support in accordance with RFC 4918 section 7.3 and annex D. Instead a lock on a non existing resource will create an empty file locked with a regular lock. (remm) 
*   ![Image 342: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Rewrite implementation of WebDAV shared locks to comply with RFC 4918. (remm) 
*   ![Image 343: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Implement WebDAV `If` header using code from the Apache Jackrabbit project. (remm) 
*   ![Image 344: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add `PropertyStore` interface in the WebDAV Servlet, to allow implementation of dead properties storage. The store used can be configured using the `propertyStore` init parameter of the WebDAV servlet by specifying the class name of the store. A simple non persistent implementation is used if no custom store is configured. (remm) 
*   ![Image 345: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Implement WebDAV `PROPPATCH` method using the newly added `PropertyStore`, and update `PROPFIND` to support it. (remm) 
*   ![Image 346: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Cache not found results when searching for web application class loader resources. This addresses performance problems caused by components such as `java.sql.DriverManager` which, in some circumstances, will search for the same class repeatedly. In a large web application this can cause performance problems. The size of the cache can be controlled via the new `notFoundClassResourceCacheSize` on the StandardContext. (markt) 
*   ![Image 347: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Stop after `INITIALIZED` state should be a noop since it is possible for subcomponents to be in `FAILED` after init. (remm) 
*   ![Image 348: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix incorrect web resource cache size calculations when there are concurrent `PUT` and `DELETE` requests for the same resource. (markt) 
*   ![Image 349: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add debug logging for the web resource cache so the current size can be tracked as resources are added and removed. (markt) 
*   ![Image 350: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Replace legacy WebDAV `opaquelocktoken:` scheme for lock tokens with `urn:uuid:` as recommended by RFC 4918, and remove `secret` init parameter. (remm) 
*   ![Image 351: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Concurrent reads and writes (e.g. `GET` and `PUT` / `DELETE`) for the same path caused corruption of the `FileResource` where some of the fields were set as if the file exists and some were set as if it does not. This resulted in inconsistent metadata. (markt) 
*   ![Image 352: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69415](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69415): Ensure that the `ExpiresFilter` only sets cache headers on `GET` and `HEAD` requests. Also skip requests where the application has set 
```
Cache-Control:
        no-store
```
. (markt) 
*   ![Image 353: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69419](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69419): Improve the performance of `ServletRequest.getAttribute()` when there are multiple levels of nested includes. Based on a patch provided by John Engebretson. (markt) 
*   ![Image 354: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) All applications to send an early hints informational response by calling `HttpServletResponse.sendError()` with a status code of 103. (schultz) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 355: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Return null SSL session id on zero length byte array returned from the SSL implementation. (remm) 
*   ![Image 356: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Skip OpenSSLConf with BoringSSL since it is unsupported. (remm) 
*   ![Image 357: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Create the `HttpParser` in `Http11Processor` if it is not present on the `AbstractHttp11Protocol` to provide better lifecycle robustness for regular HTTP/1.1. The new behavior was introduced on a previous refactoring to improve HTTP/2 performance. (remm) 
*   ![Image 358: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)`OpenSSLContext` will now throw a `KeyManagementException` if something is known to have gone wrong in the `init` method, which is the behavior documented by `javax.net.ssl.SSLContext.init`. This makes error handling more consistent. (remm) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 359: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add back tag release method as deprecated in the runtime for compat with old generated code. (remm) 
*   ![Image 360: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69399](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69399): Fix regression caused by the improvement [69333](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69333) which caused the tag `release` to be called when using tag pooling, and to be skipped when not using it. Patch submitted by Michal Sobkiewicz. (remm) 
*   ![Image 361: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69381](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69381): Improve method lookup performance in expression language. When the required method has no arguments there is no need to consider casting or coercion and the method lookup process can be simplified. Based on pull request [#770](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/770) by John Engebretson. (markt) 
*   ![Image 362: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69382](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69382): Improve the performance of the JSP include action by re-using results of relatively expensive method calls in the generated code rather than repeating them. Patch provided by John Engebretson. (markt) 
*   ![Image 363: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69398](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69398): Avoid unnecessary object allocation in `PageContextImpl`. Based on a suggestion by John Engebretson. (markt) 
*   ![Image 364: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69406](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69406): When using `StringInterpreterEnum`, do not throw an `IllegalArgumentException` when an invalid `Enum` is encountered. Instead, resolve the value at runtime. Patch provided by John Engebretson. (markt) 
*   ![Image 365: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69429](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69429): Optimise EL evaluation of method parameters for methods that do not accept any parameters. Patch provided by John Engebretson. (markt)

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 383: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69316](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69316): Ensure that `FastHttpDateFormat#getCurrentDate()` (used to generate Date headers for HTTP responses) generates the correct string for the given input. Prior to this change, the output may have wrong by one second in some cases. Pull request [#751](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/751) provided by Chenjp. (markt)

*   ![Image 386: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve HTTP/2 handling of trailer fields for requests. Trailer fields no longer need to be recieved before the headers of the subsequent stream nor are trailer fields for an in progress stream swallowed if the Connector is paused before the trailer fields are received. (markt)

This could lead to incorrect processing times appearing in the access log. (markt)

### 2024-09-10 Tomcat 9.0.94 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 398: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve performance of `ApplicationHttpRequest.parseParameters()`. Based on sample code and test cases provided by John Engebretson. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 399: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct a regression in the fix for non-blocking reads of chunked request bodies that caused `InputStream.available()` to return a non-zero value when there was no data to read. In some circumstances this could cause a blocking read to block waiting for more data rather than return the data it had already received. (markt) 
*   ![Image 400: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add a new attribute `cookiesWithoutEquals` to the `Rfc6265CookieProcessor`. The default behaviour is unchanged. (markt)

*   ![Image 402: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69301](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69301): Fix trailer headers replacing non-trailer headers when writing response headers to the access log. Based on a patch and test case provided by hypnoce. (markt) 
*   ![Image 403: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69302](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69302): If an HTTP/2 client resets a stream before the request body is fully written, ensure that any `ReadListener` is notified via a call to `ReadListener.onErrror()`. ### 2024-08-06 Tomcat 9.0.93 (remm)

#### Coyote

### not released Tomcat 9.0.92 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 421: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for RFC 8297 (Early Hints). Applications can use this feature by casting the `HttpServletResponse` to `org.apache.catalina.connector.Reponse` and then calling the method `void sendEarlyHints()`. This method will be added to the Servlet API (removing the need for the cast) in Servlet 6.2 onwards. (markt) 
*   ![Image 422: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69214](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69214): Do not reject a CORS request that uses POST but does not include a `content-type` header. Tomcat now correctly processes this as a simple CORS request. Based on a patch suggested by thebluemountain. (markt) 
*   ![Image 423: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Refactor `SpnegoAuthenticator` so it uses `Subject.callAs()` rather than `Subject.doAs()` when the available. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 424: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add OpenSSL integration using the FFM API rather than Tomcat Native. OpenSSL support may be enabled by adding the `org.apache.catalina.core.OpenSSLLifecycleListener` listener on the `Server` element when using Java 22 or later. (remm) 
*   ![Image 425: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that HTTP/2 stream input buffers are only created when there is a request body to be read. (markt) 
*   ![Image 426: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor creation of HttpParser instances from the Processor level to the Protocol level since the parser configuration depends on the protocol and the parser is, otherwise, stateless. (markt) 
*   ![Image 427: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Align HTTP/2 with HTTP/1.1 and recycle the container internal request and response processing objects by default. This behaviour can be controlled via the new `discardRequestsAndResponses` attribute on the HTTP/2 upgrade protocol. (markt) 

#### jdbc-pool

*   ![Image 428: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69206](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69206): Ensure statements returned from `Statement` methods `executeQuery()`, `getResultSet()` and `getGeneratedKeys()` are correctly wrapped before being returned to the caller. Based on pull request [#742](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/742) provided by Michael Clarke. 

#### Other

*   ![Image 429: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix packaging regression with missing osgi information following addition of the `test-only` build target. (remm) 
*   ![Image 430: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update Tomcat Native to 1.3.1. (markt)

(markt) 

#### Coyote

Interfaces that are configured for point to point connections or are not currently up are now skipped. (markt) 
*   ![Image 438: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69121](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69121): Ensure that the `onComplete()` event is triggered if `AsyncListener.onError()` dispatches to a target that throws an exception. (markt)

*   ![Image 441: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that an exception in `toString()` still results in an `ELException` when an object is coerced to a String using `ExpressionFactory.coerceToType()`. (markt)

*   ![Image 443: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[69135](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=69135): When using include directives in a tag file packaged in a JAR file, ensure that context relative includes are processed correctly. (markt)

*   ![Image 460: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) The system property `org.apache.catalina.connector.RECYCLE_FACADES` will now default to `true` if not specified, which will in turn set the default value for the `discardFacades` connector attribute, thus causing facade objects to be discarded by default. *   ![Image 464: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Introduce reference counting so the `AprLifecycleListener` is more robust. This particularly targets more complex embedded configurations with multiple server instances with independent lifecycles where more than one server instance requires the `AprLifecycleListener`. (markt)

### 2024-05-07 Tomcat 9.0.89 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 478: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Deprecate and remove `sessionCounter` (replaced by the addition of the active session count and the expired session count, as a reasonable approximation) and `duplicates` (which does not represent a possible event in current implementations) statistics from the session manager. (remm) 
*   ![Image 479: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[68890](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68890) Align output encoding of JSPs in the Manager webapp with the XML declarations in those same files. (schultz) 
*   ![Image 480: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Update Basic authentication to implement the requirements of RFC 7617 including the changing of the `trimCredentials` setting which is now defaults to `false`. Note that the `trimCredentials` setting will be removed in Tomcat 11. (markt) 
*   ![Image 481: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Small performance optimization when logging cookies with no values. (schultz) 
*   ![Image 482: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct error handling for asynchronous requests. If the application performs an dispatch during `AsyncListener.onError()` the dispatch is now performed rather than completing the request using the error page mechanism. (markt) 
*   ![Image 483: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix WebDAV lock null (locks for non existing resources) thread safety and removal. (remm) 
*   ![Image 484: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add periodic checking for WebDAV locks expiration. (remm) 
*   ![Image 485: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Extend `Asn1Parser` to parse `UTF8String`s. (michaelo) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 486: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Align non-secure and secure writes with NIO and skip the write attempt when there are no bytes to be written. (markt) 
*   ![Image 487: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Allow any positive value for `socket.unlockTimeout`. If a negative or zero value is configured, the default of `250ms` will be used. (mark) 
*   ![Image 488: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Reduce the time spent waiting for the connector to unlock. The previous default of 10s was noticeably too long for cases where the unlock has failed. The wait time is now 100ms plus twice `socket.unlockTimeout`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 489: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that the `onAllDataRead()` event is triggered when the request body uses chunked encoding and is read using non-blocking IO. (markt) 
*   ![Image 490: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[68934](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68934): Add debug logging in the latch object when exceeding `maxConnections`. (remm) 
*   ![Image 491: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Refactor trailer field handling to use a `MimeHeaders` instance to store trailer fields. (markt) 
*   ![Image 492: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that multiple instances of the same trailer field are handled correctly. (markt) 
*   ![Image 493: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix non-blocking reads of chunked request bodies. (markt) 
*   ![Image 494: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When an invalid HTTP response header was dropped, an off-by-one error meant that the first header in the response was also dropped. Fix based on pull request [#710](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/710) by foremans. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 495: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for specifying Java 23 (with the value `23`) as the compiler source and/or compiler target for JSP compilation. If used with an Eclipse JDT compiler version that does not support these values, a warning will be logged and the default will used. (markt) 

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 497: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[68884](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68884): Reduce the write timeout when writing WebSocket close messages for abnormal closes. The timeout defaults to 50 milliseconds and may be controlled using the `org.apache.tomcat.websocket.ABNORMAL_SESSION_CLOSE_SEND_TIMEOUT` property in the user properties collection associated with the WebSocket session. *   ![Image 510: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Add `highConcurrencyStatus` attribute to the `SemaphoreValve` to optionally allow the valve to return an error status code to the client when a permit cannot be acquired from the semaphore. (remm) 
*   ![Image 511: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add checking of the "age" of the running Tomcat instance since its build-date to the SecurityListener, and log a warning if the server is old. (schultz) 
*   ![Image 512: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When using the `AsyncContext`, throw an `IllegalStateException`, rather than allowing an `NullPointerException`, if an attempt is made to use the `AsyncContext` after it has been recycled. (markt)

Based upon a suggestion by Markus Wolfe. (schultz)

*   ![Image 517: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add `threadsMaxIdleTime` attribute to the endpoint, to allow configuring the amount of time before an internal executor will scale back to the configured `minSpareThreads` size. (remm) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 518: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Handle the case where the JSP engine forwards a request/response to a Servlet that uses an `OutputStream` rather than a `Writer`. This was triggering an `IllegalStateException` on code paths where there was a subsequent attempt to obtain a `Writer`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 519: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correctly handle the case where a tag library is packaged in a JAR file and the web application is deployed as a WAR file rather than an unpacked directory. (markt) 
*   ![Image 520: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Prevent the web application's ClassLoader from being pinned by the JSP compiler if an application uses a custom XMLInputFactory. Based upon a suggestion from Simon Niederberger. (schultz)

### 2024-03-14 Tomcat 9.0.87 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 527: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Minor performance improvement for building filter chains. Based on ideas from pull request [#702](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/702) by Luke Miao. (remm) 
*   ![Image 528: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Align error handling for `Writer` and `OutputStream`. Ensure use of either once the response has been recycled triggers a `NullPointerException` provided that `discardFacades` is configured with the default value of `true`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 529: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[68692](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68692): The standard thread pool implementations that are configured using the `Executor` element now implement `ExecutorService` for better support NIO2. (remm) 
*   ![Image 530: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[68495](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68495): When restoring a saved POST request after a successful FORM authentication, ensure that neither the URI, the query string nor the protocol are corrupted when restoring the request body. (markt) 
*   ![Image 531: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[68721](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68721): Workaround a possible cause of duplicate class definitions when using `ClassFileTransformer`s and the transformation of a class also triggers the loading of the same class. (markt) 
*   ![Image 532: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) The rewrite valve should not do a rewrite if the output is identical to the input. (remm) 
*   ![Image 533: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Add a new `valveSkip` (or `VS`) rule flag to the rewrite valve to allow skipping over the next valve in the Catalina pipeline. (remm) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 534: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve the HTTP/2 stream prioritisation process. If a stream uses all of the connection windows and still has content to write, it will now be added to the backlog immediately rather than waiting until the write attempt for the remaining content. (markt) 
*   ![Image 535: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct a regression in the support for user provided `SSLContext` instances that broke the `org.apache.catalina.security.TLSCertificateReloadListener`. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 536: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for specifying Java 22 (with the value `22`) as the compiler source and/or compiler target for JSP compilation. If used with an Eclipse JDT compiler version that does not support these values, a warning will be logged and the default will used. (markt) 

#### Cluster

*   ![Image 537: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid updating request count stats on async. (remm) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 538: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to French translations. (remm) 
*   ![Image 539: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Japanese translations by tak7iji. (markt) 
*   ![Image 540: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[57130](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=57130): Allow digest.(sh|bat) to accept password from a file or stdin. (csutherl/schultz) 

### 2024-02-19 Tomcat 9.0.86 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 541: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct JPMS and OSGi meta-data for `tomcat-enbed-core.jar` by removing reference to `org.apache.catalina.ssi` package that is no longer included in the JAR. Based on pull request [#684](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/684) by Jendrik Johannes. (markt) 
*   ![Image 542: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix ServiceBindingPropertySource so that trailing `\r\n` sequences are correctly removed from files containing property values when configured to do so. Bug identified by Coverity Scan. (markt) 
*   ![Image 543: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add improvements to the CSRF prevention filter including the ability to skip adding nonces for resource name and subtree URL patterns. (schultz) 
*   ![Image 544: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Review usage of debug logging and downgrade trace or data dumping operations from debug level to trace. (remm) 
*   ![Image 545: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[68089](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68089): Further improve the performance of request attribute access for `ApplicationHttpRequest` and `ApplicationRequest`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 546: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[68559](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68559): Allow asynchronous error handling to write to the response after an error during asynchronous processing. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 547: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Make asynchronous error handling more robust. Ensure that once a connection is marked to be closed, further asynchronous processing cannot change that. (markt) 
*   ![Image 548: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Make asynchronous error handling more robust. Ensure that once the call to `AsyncListener.onError()` has returned to the container, only container threads can access the `AsyncContext`. This protects against various race conditions that would otherwise occur if application threads continued to access the `AsyncContext`. 
*   ![Image 549: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Review usage of debug logging and downgrade trace or data dumping operations from debug level to trace. In particular, most of the HTTP/2 debug logging has been changed to trace level. (remm) 
*   ![Image 550: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add support for user provided `SSLContext` instances configured on `SSLHostConfigCertificate` instances. Based on pull request [#673](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/673) provided by Hakan Altındağ. (markt) 
*   ![Image 551: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve the Tomcat Native shutdown process to reduce the likelihood of a JVM crash during Tomcat shutdown. (markt) 
*   ![Image 552: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Partial fix for [68558](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68558): Cache the result of converting to `String` for request URI, HTTP header names and the request `Content-Type` value to improve performance by reducing repeated `byte[]` to `String` conversions. (markt) 
*   ![Image 553: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve error reporting to HTTP/2 clients for header processing errors by reporting problems at the end of the frame where the error was detected rather than at the end of the headers. (markt) 
*   ![Image 554: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Remove the remaining reference to a stream once the stream has been recycled. This makes the stream eligible for garbage collection earlier and thereby improves scalability. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 555: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[68546](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68546): Generate optimal size and types for JSP imports maps, as suggested by John Engebretson. (remm) 
*   ![Image 556: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Review usage of debug logging and downgrade trace or data dumping operations from debug level to trace. (remm) 

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 557: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct a regression in the fix for [66508](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66508) that could cause an `UpgradeProcessor` leak in some circumstances. (markt) 
*   ![Image 558: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Review usage of debug logging and downgrade trace or data dumping operations from debug level to trace. (remm) 
*   ![Image 559: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that WebSocket connection closure completes if the connection is closed when the server side has used the proprietary suspend/resume feature to suspend the connection. (markt) 

#### Web applications

*   ![Image 560: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for responses in JSON format from the examples application RequestHeaderExample. (schultz) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 561: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update Checkstyle to 10.13.0. (markt) 
*   ![Image 562: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update JSign to 6.0. (markt) 
*   ![Image 563: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Add strings for debug level messages. (remm) 
*   ![Image 564: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update Tomcat Native to 1.3.0. (markt) 
*   ![Image 565: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to French translations. (remm) 
*   ![Image 566: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvements to Japanese translations by tak7iji. (markt) 

### 2024-01-09 Tomcat 9.0.85 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 567: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif)[68378](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68378): Align extension to MIME type mappings in the global web.xml with those in httpd by adding `application/vnd.geogebra.slides` for `ggs`, `text/javascript` for `mjs` and `audio/ogg` for opus. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 568: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Refactor the `VirtualThreadExecutor` so that it can be used by the NIO2 connector which was using platform threads even when configured to use virtual threads. (markt) 
*   ![Image 569: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct a regression in the fix for [67675](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=67675) that broke TLS key file parsing for PKCS#8 format keys that do not specify an explicit pseudo-random function and rely on the default. This typically affects keys generated by OpenSSL 1.0.2. (markt) 
*   ![Image 570: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Allow multiple operations with the same name on introspected mbeans, fixing a regression caused by the introduction of a second `addSslHostConfig` method. (remm) 
*   ![Image 571: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Relax the check that the HTTP Host header is consistent with the host used in the request line, if any, to make the check case insensitive since host names are case insensitive. (markt) 
*   ![Image 572: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[68348](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68348): Add support for the partitioned attribute for cookies. (markt) 

#### Web Applications

*   ![Image 573: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[68035](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68035): Additional fix to the Manager application to enable the deployment of a web application located in a Host's `appBase` where the web application is specified by a bare (no path) WAR or directory name as shown in the documentation. (markt) 

#### Other

### 2023-11-15 Tomcat 9.0.83 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 592: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[67667](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=67667): `TLSCertificateReloadListener` prints unreadable rendering of `X509Certificate#getNotAfter()`. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 593: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) The status servlet included in the manager webapp can now output statistics as JSON, using the `JSON=true` URL parameter. (remm) 
*   ![Image 594: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Optionally allow ServiceBindingPropertySource to trim a trailing newline from a file containing a property-value. (schultz) 
*   ![Image 595: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[67793](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=67793): Ensure the original session timeout is restored after FORM authentication if the user refreshes a page during the FORM authentication process. Based on a suggestion by Mircea Butmalai. (markt) 
*   ![Image 596: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif)[67926](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=67926): `PEMFile` prints unidentifiable string representation of ASN.1 OIDs. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 597: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[66875](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66875): Ensure that setting the request attribute `jakarta.servlet.error.exception` is not sufficient to trigger error handling for the current request and response. (markt) 
*   ![Image 598: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[68054](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68054): Avoid some file canonicalization calls introduced by the fix for [65433](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65433). (remm) 
*   ![Image 599: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[68089](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=68089): Improve performance of request attribute access for `ApplicationHttpRequest` and `ApplicationRequest`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 600: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Use a 400 status code to report an error due to a bad request (e.g. an invalid trailer header) rather than a 500 status code. (markt) 
*   ![Image 601: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that an `IOException` during the reading of the request triggers always error handling, regardless of whether the application swallows the exception. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 602: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[66670](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66670): Add `SSLHostConfig#certificateKeyPasswordFile` and `SSLHostConfig#certificateKeystorePasswordFile`. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 603: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) When calling `SSLHostConfigCertificate.setCertificateKeystore(ks)`, automatically call `setCertificateKeystoreType(ks.getType())`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 604: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[67628](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=67628): Clarify how the `ciphers` attribute of the `SSLHostConfig` is used. (markt) 
*   ![Image 605: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[67666](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=67666): Ensure TLS connectors using PEM files either work with the `TLSCertificateReloadListener` or, in the rare case that they do not, log a warning on Connector start. (markt) 
*   ![Image 606: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[67675](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=67675): Support a wider range of KDF and ciphers for PEM files than the combinations supported by the JVM by default. Specifically, support the OpenSSL default of HmacSHA256 and DES-EDE3-CBC. (markt) 
*   ![Image 607: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[67927](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=67927): Reloading TLS configuration can cause the Connector to refuse new connections or the JVM to crash. (markt)
