### 2023-04-18 Tomcat 9.0.74 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 729: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65995](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65995): Implement RFC 9239 and use `text/javascript` as the media type for JavaScript rather than `application/javascript`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 730: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add an access log valve that uses a json format. Based on pull request [#539](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/539) provided by Thomas Meyer. (remm) 
*   ![Image 731: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Harden the FORM authentication process against DoS attacks by using a reduced session timeout if the FORM authentication process creates a session. The duration of this timeout is configured by the `authenticationSessionTimeout` attribute of the FORM authenticator. (markt) 
*   ![Image 732: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[66527](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66527): Correct the Javadoc for the `Tomcat.addWebapp()` methods that incorrectly stated that the `docBase` parameter could be a relative path. (markt) 
*   ![Image 733: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[66524](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66524) Correct eviction ordering in WebResource cache to be LRU as intended. (schultz) 
*   ![Image 734: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Use server.xml to reduce the default value of `maxParameterCount` from 10,000 to 1,000. If not configured in server.xml, the default remains 10,000. (markt) 
*   ![Image 735: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Update Digest authentication support to align with RFC 7616. This adds a new configuration attribute, `algorithms`, to the `DigestAuthenticator` with a default of `SHA-256,MD5`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 736: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Add support code for custom user attributes in `RealmBase`. Based on code from [#473](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/473) by Carsten Klein. (remm) 
*   ![Image 737: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Expand the set of HTTP request headers considered sensitive that should be skipped when generating a response to a `TRACE` request. This aligns with 11.0.x. (markt) 
*   ![Image 738: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[66541](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66541): Improve handling for cached resources for resources that use custom URL schemes. The scheme specific `equals()` and `hashCode()` algorithms, if present, will now be used for URLs for these resources. This addresses a potential performance issue with some OSGi custom URL schemes that can trigger potentially slow DNS lookups in some configurations. Based on a patch provided by Tom Whitmore. (markt) 
*   ![Image 739: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When using a custom session manager deployed as part of the web application, avoid `ClassNotFoundException`s when validating session IDs extracted from requests. (markt) 
*   ![Image 740: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[66543](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66543): Give `StandardContext#fireRequestDestroyEvent` its own log message. (fschumacher)

*   ![Image 742: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Make the server utility executor available to webapps using a Servlet context attribute named `org.apache.tomcat.util.threads.ScheduledThreadPoolExecutor`. (remm)

(markt)

### 2022-11-14 Tomcat 9.0.69 (remm)

*   ![Image 814: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[66209](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66209): Add a configuration option to allow bloom filters used to index JAR files to be retained for the lifetime of the web application. Prior to this addition, the indexes were always flushed by the periodic calls to `WebResourceRoot.gc()`. As part of this addition, configuration of archive indexing moves from `Context` to `WebResourceRoot`. Based on a patch provided by Rahul Jaisimha. (markt)

(markt)

*   ![Image 937: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65736](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65736): Disable the `forceString` option for the JNDI `BeanFactory` and replace it with an automatic search for an alternative setter with the same name that accepts a `String`. *   ![Image 938: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif)[65853](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65853): Refactor the `CsrfPreventionFilter` to make it easier for sub-classes to modify the nonce generation and storage. Based on suggestions by Marvin Fröhlich. (markt) 
*   ![Image 939: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65991](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65991): Avoid NPE with `SSLAuthenticator` when `boundOnInit` is used on a connector, during the check for client certificate authentication availability. (remm) 
*   ![Image 940: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[66009](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66009): Use `getSubjectX500Principal().toString()` rather than `getSubjectX500Principal().getName(...)` to retrieve a certificate DN, to match the output of the deprecated `getSubjectDN().getName()` that was used previously. (remm) 
*   ![Image 941: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Revert the change in 9.0.59 that added a mapping of `Shift_JIS` for the `ja` locale to the default mappings used by `ServletResponse.setLocale()` as it caused regressions for applications using UTF-8. (markt) 
*   ![Image 942: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Provide a property source that sources values from Kubernetes service bindings. Pull request [#512](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/512) provided by Sumit Kulhadia and Gareth Evans. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 943: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[#501](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/501): Add new `maxHttpRequestHeaderSize` and `maxHttpResponseHeaderSize` attributes which allow setting the maximum HTTP header sizes independently. If not specified, the value of the `maxHttpHeaderSize` connector attribute will be used. Submitted by Zhongming Hua. (remm) 
*   ![Image 944: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) The root cause of the Linux kernel duplicate accept bug has been identified along with the version of the kernel that includes the fix. The error message displayed when this bug occurs has been updated to reflect this new information and to advise users to update to a version of the OS that uses kernel 5.10 or later. Thanks to Christopher Gual for the research into this issue. (markt) 
*   ![Image 945: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[66023](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66023): Improve the fix for [65726](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65726) and support HTTP upgrade with a request body for a wider set of use cases. (markt) 
*   ![Image 946: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for encrypted PKCS#1 formatted private keys when configuring the internal, in memory key store. Based on [#511](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/511). (jfclere/markt) 
*   ![Image 947: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Remove the `prestartminSpareThreads` attribute of the `StandardThreadExecutor` since all core threads are always started by default making this attribute meaningless. Pull request [#510](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/pull/510) provided by Aooohan. (markt) 

#### Webapps

*   ![Image 948: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[66008](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=66008): In the documentation web application, clarify the recommendation for the use the `trimSpaces` option for Jasper in production environments. (markt) 
*   ![Image 949: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Update the documentation web application to state that the `EncryptInterceptor` does not provide sufficient protection to run Tomcat clustering over an untrusted network. This is CVE-2022-29885. (markt)

(markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1055: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve error handling if APR/Native fails to attach TLS capabilities to a TLS enabled client connection. (markt)

*   ![Image 1060: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Refactor APR/native connector shutdown to remove a potential source of JVM crashes on shutdown when sendfile is used. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1061: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When an error occurs that triggers a stream reset, ensure that the first `RST` frame sent to the client is the one associated with the error that triggered the reset. (markt)

(markt)

*   ![Image 1064: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid a potential deadlock during the concurrent processing of incoming HTTP/2 frames for a stream and that stream being reset. (markt)

### 2021-09-10 Tomcat 9.0.53 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1096: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Enable Tomcat to start if an (old) XML parser is configured that does not support `allow-java-encodings`. A warning will be logged if such an XML parser is detected. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1097: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Change the behaviour of custom error pages. If an error occurs after the response is committed, once the custom error page content has been added to the response the connection is now closed immediately rather than closed cleanly. i.e. the last chunk that marks the end of the response body is no longer sent. This acts as an additional signal to the client that the request experienced an error. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1098: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65479](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65479): When handling requests using JASPIC authentication, ensure that `PasswordValidationCallback.getResult()` returns the result of the password validation rather than always returning `false`. ### not released Tomcat 9.0.51 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1126: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65433](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65433): Correct a regression in the fix for [65397](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65397) where a `StringIndexOutOfBoundsException` could be triggered if the canonical path of the target of a symlink was shorter than the canonical path of the directory in which the symlink had been created. Patch provided by Cedomir Igaly. (markt)

*   ![Image 1128: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) To avoid unnecessary cache revalidation, do not add an HTTP `Expires` header when setting adding an HTTP header of `CacheControl: private`. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1129: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When writing an HTTP/2 response via sendfile (only enabled when `useAsyncIO` is true) the connection flow control window was sometimes ignored leading to various error conditions. sendfile now checks both the stream and connection flow control windows before writing. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1130: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add debug logging for writing an HTTP/2 response via sendfile. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1131: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct bugs in the HTTP/2 connection flow control management that meant it was possible for a connection to stall waiting for a connection flow control window update that had already arrived. Any streams on that connection that were trying to write when this happened would time out. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1132: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65448](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65448): When using TLS with NIO, it was possible for a blocking response write to hang just before the final TLS packet associated with the response until the connection timed out at which point the final packet would be sent and the connection closed. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1133: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65454](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65454): Fix a race condition that could result in a delay to a new request. The new request could be queued to wait for an existing request to finish processing rather than the thread pool creating a new thread to process the new request. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1134: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65460](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65460): Correct a regression introduced in the previous release in the change to reduce the number of small HTTP/2 window updates sent for streams. A logic error meant that small window updates for the connection were dropped. This meant that the connection flow window slowly reduced over time until nothing could be sent. (markt) 

#### Web applications

*   ![Image 1135: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65404](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65404): Correct a regression in the fix for [63362](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63362) that caused the server status page in the Manager web application to be truncated if HTTP upgrade was used such as when starting a WebSocket connection. (markt)

### not released Tomcat 9.0.49 (remm)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1142: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor the `RemoteIpValve` to use the common utility method for list to comma separated string conversion. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1143: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor `JNDIRealm$JNDIConnection` so its fields are accessible to sub-classes of `JNDIRealm`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1144: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix serialization warnings in `UserDatabasePrincipal` reported by SpotBugs. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1145: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65397](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65397): Calls to `ServletContext.getResourcePaths()` no longer include symbolic links in the results unless `allowLinking` has been set to `true`. If a resource is skipped because of this change, a warning will be logged as this typically indicates a configuration issue. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1146: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65368](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65368): Improve handling of clean closes of inbound TLS connections. Treat them the same way as clean closes of non-TLS connections rather than as unknown errors. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1147: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Modify the HTTP/2 connector not to sent small updates for stream flow control windows to the user agent as, depending on how the user agent is written, this may trigger small writes from the user agent that in turn trigger the overhead protection. Small updates for stream flow control windows are now combined with subsequent flow control window updates for that stream to ensure that all stream flow control window updates sent from Tomcat are larger than `overheadWindowUpdateThreshold`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1148: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add additional debug logging to track the current state of the HTTP/2 overhead count that Tomcat uses to detect and close potentially malicious connections. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1149: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Many HTTP/2 requests from browsers will trigger one overhead frame and one non-overhead frame. Change the overhead calculation so that a non-overhead frame reduces the current overhead count by 2 rather than 1. This means that, over time, the overhead count for a well-behaved connection will trend downwards. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1150: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Change the initial HTTP/2 overhead count from `-10` to `-10 * overheadCountFactor`. This means that, regardless of the value chosen for `overheadCountFactor`, when a connection opens 10 overhead frames in a row will be required to trigger the overhead protection. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1151: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Increase the default `overheadCountFactor` from `1` to `10` and change the reduction in overhead count for a non-overhead frame from `-2` to `-20`. This allows for a larger range (0-20) to be used for `overheadCountFactor` providing for finer-grained control. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1152: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Modify the parsing of HTTP header values that use the `1#token` to ignore empty elements as per RFC 7230 section 7 instead of treating the presence of empty elements as an error. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1153: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Expand the unit tests for `HttpServlet.doHead()` and correct the flushing of the response buffer. The buffer used to behave as if it was one byte smaller than the configured size. The buffer was flushed (and the response committed if required) when the buffer was full. The buffer is now flushed (and the response committed if required) if the buffer is full and there is more data to write. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1154: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix an issue where concurrent HTTP/2 writes (or concurrent reads) to the same connection could hang and eventually timeout when async IO was enabled (it is enabled by default). (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 1155: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65390](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65390): Correct a regression in the fix for [65124](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65124) and restore code that was removed in error leading to JSP compilation failures in some circumstances. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1156: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update to the Eclipse JDT compiler 4.20. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1157: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for specifying Java 17 (with the value `17`) as the compiler source and/or compiler target for JSP compilation. If used with an Eclipse JDT compiler version that does not support these values, a warning will be logged and the latest supported version will used. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1158: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65377](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65377): Update the Java code generation for JSPs not to use the boxed primitive constructors as they have been deprecated in Java 9 and marked for future removal in Java 16. `valueOf()` is now used instead. (markt) 

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 1159: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor the `DigestAuthenticator` to reuse a shared `SecureRandom` instance rather than create a new one to generate the `cnonce` if required. (markt) 

#### Web applications

*   ![Image 1160: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65385](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65385): Correct the link in the documentation web application the Maven Central repository. (markt) 

#### Other

PR provided by MCMicS. (markt)

Based on a pull request by Jean-Louis Monteiro. (markt)

Pull request provided by tianshuang. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1179: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[62912](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=62912): Don't mutate an application provided content header if it does not contain a charset. Also remove the outdated workaround for the buggy Adobe Reader 9 plug-in for IE. (markt)

(markt)

Submitted by Thomas, and verified the fix is present in the donated hpack code in a further update. (remm)

(markt) 
*   ![Image 1195: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Remove support for the `identity` transfer encoding. The inclusion of this encoding in RFC 2616 was an error that was corrected in 2001. Requests using this transfer encoding will now receive a 501 response. (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1252: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Revert an incorrect fix for a potential resource leak that broke deployment via the Ant deploy task. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1253: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve error message for failed ConfigurationSource lookups in the Catalina implementation. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1254: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[64938](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=64938): Align the behaviour when `null` is passed to the `ServletResponse` methods `setCharacterEncoding()`, `setContentType()` and `setLocale()` with the recent clarification from the Jakarta Servlet project of the expected behaviour in these cases. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1255: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65135](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65135): Rename Context method `isParallelAnnotationScanning` to `getParallelAnnotationScanning` for consistency and ease of use in JMX descriptors. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1256: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that the `AsyncListener.onError()` event is triggered when a I/O error occurs during non-blocking I/O. There were some cases discovered where this was not happening. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1257: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Make the non-blocking I/O error handling more robust by handling the case where the application code swallows an `IOException` in `WriteListener.onWritePossible()` and `ReadListener.onDataAvailable()`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1258: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct syntax error in output of `JsonErrorReportValve`. Pull request provided by Viraj Kanwade. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1259: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Make the `StandardContext.postWorkDirectory()` protected rather than private to help users wishing to customise the default work directory behaviour. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1260: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65118](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65118): Fix a potential `NullPointerException` when pruning closed HTTP/2 streams from the connection. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1261: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid NullPointerException when a secure channel is closed before the SSL engine was initialized. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1262: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that the `ReadListener`'s `onError()` event is triggered if the client closes the connection before sending the entire request body and the server is reading the request body using non-blocking I/O. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1263: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65137](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65137): Ensure that a response is not corrupted as well as incomplete if the connection is closed before the response is fully written due to a write timeout. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1264: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Related to bug [65131](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65131), make sure all errors from OpenSSL are fully cleared, as there could be more than one error present after an operation (confirmed in the OpenSSL API documentation). (remm) 
*   ![Image 1265: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Make handling of OpenSSL read errors more robust when plain text data is reported to be available to read. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1266: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct handling of write errors during non-blocking I/O to ensure that the associated `AsyncContext` was closed down correctly. (markt)

### not released Tomcat 9.0.42 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1279: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[60781](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=60781): Escape elements in the access log that need to be escaped for the access log to be parsed unambiguously. (fschumacher/markt) 
*   ![Image 1280: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[64110](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=64110): Add support for additional TLS related request attributes that provide details of the protocols and ciphers requested by a client in the initial TLS handshake. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1281: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Let the `RemoteCIDRValve` inherit from `RequestFilterValve` and support all of its features. Especially add support for connector specific configuration using `addConnectorPort`. (rjung) 
*   ![Image 1282: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add `peerAddress` to coyote request, which contains the IP address of the direct connection peer. If a reverse proxy sits in front of Tomcat and the protocol used is AJP or HTTP in combination with the `RemoteIp(Valve|Filter)`, the peer address might differ from the `remoteAddress`. The latter then contains the address of the client in front of the reverse proxy, not the address of the proxy itself. Support for the peer address has been added to the RemoteAddrValve and RemoteCIDRValve with the new attribute `usePeerAddress`. This can be used to restrict access to Tomcat based on the reverse proxy IP address, which is especially useful to harden access to AJP connectors. The peer address can also be logged in the access log using the new `%{peer}a` syntax. (rjung) 
*   ![Image 1283: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid uncaught InaccessibleObjectException on Java 16 trying to clear references threads. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1284: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65033](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65033): Fix JNDI realm error handling when connecting to a failed server when pooling was not enabled. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1285: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65047](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65047): If the `AccessLogValve` is unable to open the access log file, include information on the current user in the associated log message (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1286: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Additional fix for [64830](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=64830) to address an edge case that could trigger request corruption with h2c connections. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1287: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[64974](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=64974): Improve handling of pipelined HTTP requests in combination with the Servlet non-blocking IO API. It was possible that some requests could get dropped. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1288: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for using Unix domain sockets for NIO when running on Java 16 or later. This uses NIO specific `unixDomainSocketPath` and `unixDomainSocketPathPermissions` attributes. Based on a PR submitted by Graham Leggett. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1289: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[65001](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=65001): Fix error handling for exceptions thrown from calls to `ReadListener` and `WriteListener`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1290: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid possible infinite loop in `OpenSSLEngine.unwrap` when the destination buffers state is changed concurrently. (remm) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 1309: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[56890](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=56890): Align the behaviour of `ServletContext.getRealPath(String path)` with the recent clarification from the Servlet specification project. If the path parameter does not start with `/` then Tomcat processes the call as if `/` is appended to the beginning of the provided path. (markt)

### 2020-11-17 Tomcat 9.0.40 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1323: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[55559](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=55559): Add a new attribute, `localJndiResource`, that allows a UserDatabaseRealm to obtain a UserDatabase instance from the local (web application) JNDI context rather than the global JNDI context. This option is only useful when the Realm is defined on the Context. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1324: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[64805](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=64805): Correct imports used by `JMXProxyServlet`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1325: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix JNDIRealm pooling problems retrying on another bad connection. Any retries are made on a new connection, just like with the single connection scenario. Also remove all connections from the pool after an error. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1326: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Remove the entry for `org.apache.tomcat.util.descriptor.tld.LocalStrings` from tomcat-embed-core's GraalVM tomcat-resource.json. It no more part of the jar since [Fix unwanted JPMS dependency of embed-core on embed-jasper](https://github.com/apache/tomcat/commit/3815b4951eb3acd30a0b77aafa75fbdb928d5782). (mgrigorov)

*   ![Image 1329: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add GraalVM config for Tomcat JNI related classes. This makes it possible to use the APR protocol in GraalVM native images. To use it add the following to the native-image arguments: `-H:JNIConfigurationResources=META-INF/native-image/org.apache.tomcat.embed/tomcat-embed-core/tomcat-jni.json` (mgrigorov)

*   ![Image 1565: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[64184](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=64184): Avoid repeated log messages if a `MemoryUserDatabase` is configured but the specified configuration file is missing. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1566: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[64189](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=64189): Expose the web application version String as a `ServletContext` attribute named `org.apache.catalina.webappVersion`. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1567: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When the NIO or APR/native connectors were configured with `useAsyncIO="true"` and a zero length read or write was performed, the read/write would time out rather than return immediately. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1568: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[64141](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=64141): If using a CA certificate, remove a default value for the truststore file when not using a JSSE configuration. (remm)

Based on a suggestion from Alejandro Anadon. (markt)

*   ![Image 1597: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Deprecate the `JmxRemoteLifecycleListener` as the features it provides are now available in the remote JMX capability included with the JRE. This listener will be removed in Tomcat 10 and may be removed from Tomcat 9.0.x some time after 2020-12-31. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1598: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[64011](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=64011): `JNDIRealm` no longer authenticates to LDAP. (michaelo)

Note that where both the container and the application provide the same SCI, it is the application provided SCI that will be used. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1600: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) SCI definitions from JARs unpacked into `WEB-INF/classes` are now handled consistently and will always be found irrespective of whether the web application defines a JAR ordering or not. (markt)

(markt)

### 2019-11-21 Tomcat 9.0.29 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1665: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Refactor JMX remote RMI registry creation. This is the fix for CVE-2019-12418. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1666: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improvement to CsrfPreventionFilter: expose the latest available nonce as a request attribute; expose the expected nonce request parameter name as a context attribute. (schultz) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1667: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[63835](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63835): Add support for Keep-Alive response header. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 1668: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct a logic bug in the `NioEndpoint` timeout handling that meant a write timeout could be handled as a read timeout. (markt) 

#### Web applications

*   ![Image 1669: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add a warning regarding potential poor performance of the HTTP and AJP connectors if `socket.txBufSize` is configured with an explicit value rather than using the JVM default. (markt) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 1670: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve OWB module based using custom shade appender. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1671: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add security filter in OWB module in addition to the valve for more flexibility. (remm) 

### not released Tomcat 9.0.28 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1672: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Bad paths for URIs can cause exceptions on Windows due to its path separator, so wrap using an IOException. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1673: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63832](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63832): Properly mark container as FAILED when a JVM error occurs on stop. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1674: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add more details on the usage of `RewriteMap` functionality in the `RewriteValve`. (fschumacher) 
*   ![Image 1675: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63836](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63836) Ensure that references to the Host object are cleared once the Host instance is destroyed. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1676: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that, when static resource caching is enabled for a web application, all access to static files (including JSP files) goes via the cache so that a consistent view of the static files is seen. Prior to this change it was possible to see an updated last modified time but the content would be that prior to the modification. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1677: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif)[63905](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63905) Clean up Tomcat CSS. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 1678: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63909](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63909): When the `ExpiresFilter` is used without a default and the response is served by the Default Servlet, ensure that the filter processes the response if the Default Servlet sets a 304 (Not Found) status code. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1679: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that `ServletRequest.isAsyncStarted()` returns `false` once `AsyncContext.complete()` or `AsyncContext.dispatch()` has been called during `AsyncListener.onTimeout()` or `AsyncListener.onError()`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1680: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63816](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63816) and [63817](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63817): Correctly handle I/O errors after asynchronous processing has been started but before the container thread that started asynchronous processing has completed processing the current request/response. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1681: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63825](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63825): When processing the `Expect` and `Connection` HTTP headers looking for a specific token, be stricter in ensuring that the exact token is present. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1682: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63829](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63829): Improve the check of the `Content-Encoding` header when looking to see if Tomcat is serving pre-compressed content. Ensure that only a full token is matched and that the match is case insensitive. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1683: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63864](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63864): Refactor parsing of the `transfer-encoding` request header to use the shared parsing code and reduce duplication. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1684: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63865](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63865): Add `Unset` option to same-site cookies and pass through `None` value if set by user. Patch provided by John Kelly. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1685: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63879](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63879): Remove stack trace from debug logging on socket wrapper close. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1686: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Add connection tracking on the connector endpoint to remove excessive concurrency in the protocol handler when maintaining an association between the socket wrapper and its current processor. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1687: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63894](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63894): Ensure that the configured values for `certificateVerification` and `certificateVerificationDepth` are correctly passed to the OpenSSL based SSLEngine implementation. (remm/markt) 
*   ![Image 1688: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve cleanup after errors when setting socket options. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1689: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63859](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63859): Do not perform a blocking read after a `CPING` message is received by the AJP connector because, if the JK Connector is configured with `ping_mode="I"`, the `CPING` message will not always be followed by the start of a request. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1690: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Properly calculate all dynamic parts of the ErrorReportValve response on the fly in `org.apache.coyote.http2.TestHttp2InitialConnection`. (michaelo) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 1691: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63897](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63897): Capture the timestamp of a JSP for the purposes of modification tracking before the JSP is compiled to prevent a race condition if the JSP is modified during compilation. Patch provided by Karl von Randow. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1692: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a race condition that could mean changes to a modified JSP were not visible to end users. (markt) 

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 1693: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63913](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63913): Wrap any `NullPointerException`s throw by the `Inflater` or `Deflater` used by the `PerMessageDeflate` extension in an `IOException` so that the error can be caught and handled by the WebSocket error handling mechanism. (markt) 

#### Web applications

*   ![Image 1694: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct the description of the default value for the server attribute in the security How-To. (markt) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 1695: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63815](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63815): Quote the use of `CATALINA_OPTS` and `JAVA_OPTS` when used in shell scripts to avoid the expansion of `*`. Note that any newlines present in `CATALINA_OPTS` and/or `JAVA_OPTS` will no longer removed. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1696: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63826](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63826): Remove `commons-daemon-native.tar.gz` and `tomcat-native.tar.gz` from the binary zip distributions for Windows since compiled versions of those components are already included within the zip distributions. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1697: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63838](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63838): Suppress reflexive access warnings when running the unit tests on the command line. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1698: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add missing charsets from the HPE JVM on HP-UX to pass unit tests in `org.apache.tomcat.util.buf.TestCharsetCache`. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 1699: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update the CXF module to Apache CXF 3.3.4. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1700: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Expand the coverage and quality of the French translations provided with Apache Tomcat. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1701: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Expand the coverage and quality of the Japanese translations provided with Apache Tomcat. Patch provided by motohashi.yuki. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1702: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Expand the coverage and quality of the Simplified Chinese translations provided with Apache Tomcat. Contributions provided by rpo130, Mason Shen, leeyazhou, winsonzhao, qingshi huang, Lay, Shucheng Hou and Yanming Zhou. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1703: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Expand the coverage and quality of the Brazilian Portuguese translations provided with Apache Tomcat. Patch provided by Danielamorais. (markt) 

### 2019-10-11 Tomcat 9.0.27 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1704: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct a regression introduced in 9.0.25 that prevented configuration files from being loaded from the class path. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1705: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Use URL safe base 64 encoding rather than standard base 64 encoding when generating or parsing the `HTTP2-Settings` header as part of an HTTP upgrade to `h2c` as required by RFC 7540. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1706: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63765](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63765): NIO2 should try to unwrap after TLS handshake to avoid edge cases. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1707: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63766](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63766): Ensure Processor objects are recycled when processing an HTTP upgrade connection that terminates before processing switches to the Processor for the upgraded protocol. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1708: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a memory leak introduced by the HTTP/2 timeout refactoring in 9.0.23 that could occur when HTTP/2 or WebSocket was used. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 1709: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update to the Eclipse JDT compiler 4.13. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1710: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add GraalVM specific ELResolver to avoid BeanInfo use in BeanElResolver if possible, as it needs manual reflection configuration. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1711: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63781](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63781): When performing various checks related to the visibility of classes, fields an methods in the EL implementation, also check that the containing module has been exported. (markt) 

#### Web Socket

*   ![Image 1712: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63753](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63753): Ensure that the `Host` header in a Web Socket HTTP upgrade request only contains a port if a non-default port is being used. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1713: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When running on Java 9 and above, don't attempt to instantiate WebSocket Endpoints found in modules that are not exported. (markt) 

#### Web Applications

*   ![Image 1714: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add base GraalVM documentation. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1715: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add Javadoc for the Common Annotations API implementation. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1716: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct various typos in the comments, error messages and Javadoc. Patch provided by 康智冬. (markt) 

#### jdbc-pool

*   ![Image 1717: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When connections are validated without an explicit validation query, ensure that any transactions opened by the validation process are committed. Patch provided by Pascal Davoust. (markt) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 1718: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Deprecate `org.apache.tomcat.util.compat.TLS`. Its functionality was only used for unit tests in `org.apache.tomcat.util.net.TesterSupport` and has been moved there. (rjung) 
*   ![Image 1719: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63759](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63759): When installing Tomcat with the Windows installer, grant sufficient privileges to enable the uninstaller to execute when user account control is active. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1720: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Use a build property to define the minimum supported Java version and use that build property to reduce the number of edits required to update the minimum supported Java version. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1721: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update the OWB module to Apache OpenWebBeans 2.0.12. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1722: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update the CXF module to Apache CXF 3.3.3. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1723: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif)[63767](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63767): Update to Commons Daemon 1.2.2. This corrects a regression in Commons Daemon 1.2.0 and 1.2.1 that caused the Windows Service to crash on start when running on an operating system that had not been fully updated. (markt)

### not released Tomcat 9.0.25 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 1725: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid a possible `InvalidPathException` when obtaining a URI for a configuration file. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1726: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63684](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63684): `Wrapper` never passed to `RealmBase.hasRole()` for given security constraints. (michaelo) 
*   ![Image 1727: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63740](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63740): Ensure configuration files are loaded correctly when a `Host` is configured with an `xmlBase`. Patch provided by uk4sx. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1728: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid a potential `NullPointerException` on Service stop if a Service is embedded directly (i.e. with no Server) in an application and JNDI is enabled. Patch provided by S. Ali Tokmen. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1729: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add a new `PropertySource` implementation, `EnvironmentPropertySource`, that can be used to do property replacement in configuration files with environment variables. Based on a pull request provided by Thomas Meyer. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1730: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63682](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63682): Fix a potential hang when using the asynchronous Servlet API to write the response body and the stream and/or connection window reaches 0 bytes in size. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1731: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63690](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63690): Use the average of the current and previous sizes when calculating overhead for HTTP/2 `DATA` and `WINDOW_UPDATE` frames to avoid false positives as a result of client side buffering behaviour that causes a small percentage of non-final DATA frames to be smaller than expected. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1732: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63706](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63706): Avoid NPE accessing https port with plaintext. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1733: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct typos in the names of the configuration attributes `overheadDataThreshold` and `overheadWindowUpdateThreshold`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1734: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) If the HTTP/2 connection requires an initial window size larger than the default, send a WINDOW_UPDATE to increase the flow control window for the connection so that the initial size of the flow control window for the connection is consistent with the increased value. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1735: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63710](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63710): When using HTTP/2, ensure that a `content-length` header is not set for those responses with status codes that do not permit one. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1736: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63737](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63737): Correct various issues when parsing the `accept-encoding` header to determine if gzip encoding is supported including only parsing the first header found. (markt)

*   ![Image 1763: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid a `NullPointerException` in the `CrawlerSessionManagerValve` if no ROOT Context is deployed and a request does not map to any of the other deployed Contexts. Patch provided by Jop Zinkweg. (markt)

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 1765: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor the APR poller to always use a single pollset now that the Windows operating systems that required multiple smaller pollsets to be used are no longer supported. (markt)

*   ![Image 1833: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Remove `acceptorThreadCount` Connector attribute, one accept thread is sufficient. As documented, value `2` was the only other sensible value, but without and impact beyond certain microbenchmarks. (remm)

*   ![Image 1874: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[63361](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63361): Add a new method (`Registry.disableRegistry()`) that can be used to disable JMX registration of Tomcat components providing it is called before the first component is registered. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1875: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid `OutOfMemoryError`s and `ArrayIndexOutOfBoundsException`s when accessing large files via the default servlet when resource caching has been disabled. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1876: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid a `NullPointerException` when a `Context` is defined in `server.xml` with a `docBase` but not the optional `path`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1877: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63333](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63333): Override the `isAvailable()` method in the `JAASRealm` so that only login failures caused by invalid credentials trigger account lock out when the `LockOutRealm` is in use. The default value is `false`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1950: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63210](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63210): Ensure that the Apache Commons DBCP 2 based default connection pool is correctly shutdown when it is no longer required. This ensures that a non-daemon thread is not left running that will prevent Tomcat from shutting down cleanly. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1951: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63213](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63213): Ensure the correct escaping of group names when searching for nested groups when the JNDIRealm is configured with `roleNested` set to `true`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1952: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63236](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63236): Use `String.intern()` as suggested by Phillip Webb to reduce memory wasted due to String duplication. This changes saves ~245k when starting a clean installation. With additional thanks to YourKit Java profiler for helping to track down the wasted memory and the root causes. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1953: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63246](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63246): Fix a potential `NullPointerException` when calling `AsyncContext.dispatch()`. (markt)

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 1968: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Remove the `STREAMS_DROP_EMPTY_MESSAGES` system property that was introduced to work-around four failing TCK tests. An alternative solution has been implemented. Sending messages via `getSendStream()` and `getSendWriter()` will now only result in messages on the wire if data is written to the `OutputStream` or `Writer`. Writing zero length data will result in an empty message. Note that sending a message via an `Encoder` may result in the message being send via `getSendStream()` or `getSendWriter()`. (markt) 

#### Web applications

*   ![Image 1969: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix messages used by Manager and Host Manager web applications. Improve wording of messages for expire sessions command. (kkolinko) 
*   ![Image 1970: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Do not add CSRF nonce parameter and suppress Referer header for external links in Manager and Host Manager web applications. (kkolinko)

*   ![Image 1994: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63002](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63002): Fix setting rewrite qsdiscard flag. (remm) 
*   ![Image 1995: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Implement the requirements of section 8.2.2 2c of the Servlet specification and prevent a web application from deploying if it has fragments with duplicate names and is configured to use relative ordering of fragments. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1996: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that the HEAD response is consistent with the GET response when `HttpServlet` is relied upon to generate the HEAD response and the GET response uses chunking. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1997: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that the `ServletOutputStream` implementation is consistent with the requirements of asynchronous I/O and that all of the write methods use a single write rather than multiple writes. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1998: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct the Javadoc for `Context.getDocBase()` and `Context.setDocBase()` and remove text that indicates that a URL may be used for the `docBase` as this has not been the case for quite some time. (markt) 
*   ![Image 1999: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Add basic health check valve. (remm) 
*   ![Image 2000: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct a bug exposed in 9.0.14 and ensure that the Tomcat terminates in a timely manner when running as a service. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2001: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Log a message when using a Connector that requires Apr without enabling the AprLifecycleListener first. (csutherl) 
*   ![Image 2002: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Utility thread count for special negative or zero values will again be based on Runtime.getRuntime().availableProcessors(). (remm) 
*   ![Image 2003: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Treat I/O errors during request body reads the same way as I/O errors during response body writes. The errors are treated as client side errors rather than server side errors and only logged at debug level. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2004: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63038](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63038): Ensure that a `ClassNotFoundException` is thrown when attempting to load a class from a corrupted JAR file. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2005: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63078](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63078): Ensure the utility thread pool is at least two, as the deployer uses a blocking pattern. (remm, markt) 
*   ![Image 2006: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Make the removal of leading and trailing whitespace from credentials passed to BASIC authentication configurable via a new attribute, `trimCredentials` on the `BasicAuthenticator`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2007: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63003](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63003): Extend the `unloadDelay` attribute on a `Context` to include in-flight asynchronous requests. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2008: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[63026](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63026): Add a new attribute, `forceDnHexEscape`, to the `JNDIRealm` that forces escaping in the String representation of a distinguished name to use the `\nn` form. This may avoid issues with realms using Active Directory which appears to be more tolerant of optional escaping when the `\nn` form is used. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2009: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid a swallowed (and therefore ignored) access failure during web application class loading when running under a `SecurityManager`. (markt)

*   ![Image 2012: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[63137](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=63137): If the resources for a web application have been configured with multiple locations mapped to `/WEB-INF/classes`, ensure that all of those locations are used when building the web application class path. Patch provided by Marcin Gołębski. (markt)

Based on a patch submitted by Thomas Meyer with testing and suggestions by Coty Sutherland. (remm) 
*   ![Image 2183: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[62507](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=62507): Ensure that JSSE based TLS connectors work correctly with a DKS keystore. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2184: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Refactor code that adds an additional header name to the `Vary` HTTP response header to use a common utility method that addresses several additional edge cases. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2185: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[62515](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=62515): When a connector is configured (via setting `bindOnInit` to `false`) to bind/unbind the server socket during start/stop, close the socket earlier in the stop process so new connections do not sit in the TCP backlog during the shutdown process only to be dropped as stop completes. In this scenario new connections will now be refused immediately. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2186: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[62526](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=62526): Correctly handle PKCS12 format key stores when the key store password is configured to be the empty string. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2187: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[62605](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=62605): Ensure `ReadListener.onDataAvailable()` is called when the initial request body data arrives after the request headers when using asynchronous processing over HTTP/2. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2188: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[62614](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=62614): Ensure that `WriteListener.onWritePossible()` is called after `isReady()` returns `false` and the window size is subsequently incremented when using asynchronous processing over HTTP/2. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 2189: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[53492](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=53492): Make the Java file generation process multi-threaded. By default, one thread will be used per core. Based on a patch by Dan Fabulich. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2190: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[62453](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=62453): Add a performance optimisation for using expressions in tags that depend on uninitialised tag attributes with implied scope. Generally, using an explicit scope with tag attributes in EL is the best way to avoid various potential performance issues. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2191: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correctly decode URL paths (`+` should not be decoded to a space in the path) in the Jasper class loader. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2192: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[62603](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=62603): Fix a potential race condition when development mode is disabled and background compilation checks are enabled. It was possible that some updates would not take effect and/or `ClassNotFoundException`s would occur. (markt) 

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 2193: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[62596](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=62596): Remove the limit on the size of the initial HTTP upgrade request used to establish the web socket connection. (markt) 

#### Web applications

(markt) 

#### Tribes

*   ![Image 2198: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct the stop order of the Channel components. It stops in the reverse order to that at startup. (kfujino) 
*   ![Image 2199: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Added new StaticMembership implementation. This implementation does not require any additional configuration of other `ChannelInterceptors`. It works only with membership service. (kfujino)

### not released Tomcat 9.0.9 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 2210: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Treat the `<mapped-name>` element of a `<env-entry>` in web.xml in the same way as the `mappedName` element of the equivalent `@Resource` annotation. Both now attempt to set the `mappedName` property of the resource. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2211: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct the processing of resources with `<injection-target>`s defined in web.xml. First look for a match using JavaBean property names and then, only if a match is not found, look for a match using fields. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2212: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When restoring a saved request with a request body after FORM authentication, ensure that calls to the `HttpServletRequest` methods `getRequestURI()`, `getQueryString()` and `getProtocol()` are not corrupted by the processing of the saved request body. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2213: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) JNDI resources that are defined with injection targets but no value are now treated as if the resource is not defined. (markt)

*   ![Image 2216: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add the `AuthenticatedUserRealm` for use with CLIENT-CERT and SPNEGO when just the authenticated user name is required. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2217: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[50175](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=50175): Add a new attribute to the standard context implementation, `skipMemoryLeakChecksOnJvmShutdown`, that allows the user to configure Tomcat to skip the memory leak checks usually performed during web application stop if that stop is triggered by a JVM shutdown. *   ![Image 2218: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[51497](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=51497): Add an option, `ipv6Canonical`, to the `AccessLogValve` that causes IPv6 addresses to be output in canonical form defined by RFC 5952. (ognjen/markt)

*   ![Image 2301: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) The OpenSSL engine SSL session will now ignore invalid accesses. (remm) 
*   ![Image 2302: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[62177](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=62177): Correct two protocol errors with HTTP/2 `PUSH_PROMISE` frames. Firstly, the HTTP/2 protocol only permits pushes to be sent on peer initiated requests. Secondly, pushes must be sent in order of increasing stream ID. These restriction were not being enforced leading to protocol errors at the client. (markt)

*   ![Image 2315: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[43866](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=43866): Add additional attributes to the Manager to provide control over which listeners are called when an attribute is added to the session when it has already been added under the same name. This is to aid clustering scenarios where `setAttribute()` is often called to signal that the attribute value has been mutated and needs to be replicated but it may not be required, or even desired, for the associated listeners to be triggered. The default behaviour has not been changed. (markt)

This check is optional but enabled by default. It may be disabled with the `allowHostHeaderMismatch` attribute of the Connector. (markt)

*   ![Image 2481: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[61424](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=61424): Avoid a possible `StackOverflowError` when running under a `SecurityManager` and using `Subject.doAs()`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2482: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) When running under Java 9 or later, and the `urlCacheProtection` option of the `JreMemoryLeakPreventionListener` is enabled, use the API added in Java 9 to only disable the caching for JAR URL connections. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2483: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[61489](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=61489): When using the CGI servlet, make the generation of command line arguments from the query string (as per section 4.4 of RFC 3875) optional and disabled by default. Based on a patch by jm009. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2484: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[61503](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=61503): This corrects a potential regression in the fix for [60940](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=60940) with an alternative solution that adds the `JarEntry` objects normally skipped by a `JarInputStream` only if those entries exist. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 2485: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) The minimum required Tomcat Native version has been increased to 1.2.14. This version includes a new API needed for correct client certificate support when using a Java connector with OpenSSL TLS implementation and support for the `SSL_CONF` OpenSSL API. (rjung) 
*   ![Image 2486: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for the OpenSSL `SSL_CONF` API when using TLS with OpenSSL implementation. It can be used by adding `OpenSSLConf` elements underneath `SSLHostConfig`. The new element contains a list of `OpenSSLConfCmd` elements, each with the attributes `name` and `value`. (rjung) 
*   ![Image 2487: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When using a Java connector in combination with the OpenSSL TLS implementation, do not configure each SSL connection object via the OpenSSLEngine. For OpenSSL the SSL object inherits its settings from the SSL_CTX which we have already configured. (rjung) 
*   ![Image 2488: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When using JSSE TLS configuration with the OpenSSL implementation and client certificates: include client CA subjects in the TLS handshake so that the client can choose an appropriate client certificate to present. (rjung) 
*   ![Image 2489: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) If an invalid option is specified for the `certificateVerification` attribute of an `SSLHostConfig` element, treat it as `required` which is the most secure / restrictive option in addition to reporting the configuration error. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2490: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve the handling of client disconnections during the TLS renegotiation handshake. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2491: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Prevent exceptions being thrown during normal shutdown of NIO connections. This enables TLS connections to close cleanly. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2492: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix possible race condition when setting IO listeners on an upgraded connection. (remm) 
*   ![Image 2493: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that the APR/native connector uses blocking I/O for TLS renegotiation. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2494: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[48655](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=48655): Enable Tomcat to shutdown cleanly when using sendfile, the APR/native connector and a multi-part download is in progress. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2495: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58244](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58244): Handle the case when OpenSSL resumes a TLS session using a ticket and the full client certificate chain is not available. In this case the client certificate without the chain will be presented to the application. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2496: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve the warning message when JSSE and OpenSSL configuration styles are mixed on the same `SSLHostConfig`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2497: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[61415](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=61415): Fix TLS renegotiation with OpenSSL based connections and session caching. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2498: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Delay checking that the configured attributes for an `SSLHostConfig` instance are consistent with the configured SSL implementation until `Connector` start to avoid incorrect warnings when the SSL implementation changes during initialisation. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2499: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[61450](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=61450): Fix default key alias algorithm. (remm) 
*   ![Image 2500: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[61451](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=61451): Correct a regression in the fix to enable the use of Java key stores that contained multiple keys that did not all have the same password. The regression broke support for any key store that did not store keys in PKCS #8 format such as hardware key stores and Windows key stores. (markt)

### not released Tomcat 9.0.0.M24 (markt)

*   ![Image 2534: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[52924](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=52924): Add support for a Tomcat specific deployment descriptor, `/WEB-INF/tomcat-web.xml`. This descriptor has an identical format to `/WEB-INF/web.xml`. The Tomcat descriptor takes precedence over any settings in `conf/web.xml` but does not take precedence over any settings in `/WEB-INF/web.xml`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2535: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[61232](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=61232): When log rotation is disabled only one separator will be used when generating the log file name. For example if the prefix is `catalina.` and the suffix is `.log` then the log file name will be `catalina.log` instead of `catalina..log`. Patch provided by Katya Stoycheva. (violetagg) 
*   ![Image 2536: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[61264](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=61264): Correct a regression in the refactoring to use `Charset` rather than `String` to store request character encoding that prevented `getReader()` throwing an `UnsupportedEncodingException` if the user agent specifies an unsupported character encoding. This significantly reduces the memory footprint of Jasper in development mode, provides a small performance improvement for error page generation and enables source quotes to continue to be provided after a Tomcat restart. This was accomplished by adding a custom permission, `org.apache.catalina.security.DeployXmlPermission`, that permits an application to use a `META-INF/context.xml` file and then granting that permission to the Manager and Host Manager. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2570: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[61173](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=61173): Polish the javadoc for `o.a.catalina.startup.Tomcat`. Patch provided by peterhansson_se. (violetagg) 
*   ![Image 2571: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) A new configuration property `crawlerIps` is added to the `o.a.catalina.valves.CrawlerSessionManagerValve`. Using this property one can specify a regular expression that will be used to identify crawlers based on their IP address. Based on a patch provided by Tetradeus. (violetagg) 
*   ![Image 2572: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[61180](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=61180): Log a warning message rather than an information message if it takes more than 100ms to initialised a `SecureRandom` instance for a web application to use to generate session identifiers. Patch provided by Piotr Chlebda. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2573: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[61185](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=61185): When an asynchronous request is dispatched via `AsyncContext.dispatch()` ensure that `getRequestURI()` for the dispatched request matches that of the original request. *   ![Image 2574: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[61197](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=61197): Ensure that the charset name used in the `Content-Type` header has exactly the same form as that provided by the application. This reverts a behavioural change in 9.0.0.M21 that caused problems for some clients. (markt)

### 2017-05-10 Tomcat 9.0.0.M21 (markt)

#### General

*   ![Image 2601: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Allow to exclude JUnit test classes using the build property `test.exclude` and document the property in BUILDING.txt. (rjung) 

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 2602: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Review those places where Tomcat re-encodes a URI or URI component and ensure that the correct encoding (path differs from query string) is applied and that the encoding is applied consistently. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2603: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Avoid a `NullPointerException` when reading attributes for a initialised HTTP connector where TLS is enabled. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2604: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Always quote the `hostName` of an `SSLHostConfig` element when using it as part of the JMX object name to avoid errors that prevent the associated TLS connector from starting if a wild card `hostName` is configured (because `*` is a reserved character for JMX object names). (markt) 
*   ![Image 2605: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update the default `URIEncoding` for a `Connector` to `UTF-8` as required by the Servlet 4.0 specification. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2606: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Switch to using `Charset` rather than `String` to store encoding settings (including for configuration and for the `Content-Type header`) to reduce the number of places the associated `Charset` needs to be looked up. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2607: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Use a more reliable mechanism for the `DefaultServlet` when determining if the current request is for custom error page or not. (markt)

*   ![Image 2609: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) If a static custom error page is specified that does not exist or cannot be read, ensure that the intended error status is returned rather than a 404 or 403. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2610: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When the WebDAV servlet is configured and an error dispatch is made to a custom error page located below `WEB-INF`, ensure that the target error page is displayed rather than a 404 response. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2611: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update the Servlet 4.0 implementation to add support for obtaining trailer fields from chunked HTTP requests. (markt)

Note that the Servlet 4.0 API is still a work in progress and further changes are likely. (markt)
