### 2016-10-10 Tomcat 9.0.0.M11 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 2842: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[59961](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59961): Add an option to the `StandardJarScanner` to control whether or not JAR Manifests are scanned for additional class path entries. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2843: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[60013](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=60013): Refactor the previous fix to align the behaviour of the Rewrite Valve with mod_rewrite. As part of this, provide an implementation for the `B` and `NE` flags and improve the handling for the `QSA` flag. Includes multiple test cases by Santhana Preethiand a patch by Tiago Oliveira. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2844: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[60087](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=60087): Refactor the web resources handling to use the Tomcat specific `war:file:...` URL protocol to refer to WAR files and their contents rather than the standard `jar:file:...` form since some components of the JRE, such as JAR verification, give unexpected results when the standard form is used. A side-effect of the refactoring is that when using packed WARs, it is now possible to reference a WAR and/or specific JARs within a WAR in the security policy file used when running under a `SecurityManager`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2845: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[60116](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=60116): Fix a problem with the rewrite valve that caused back references evaluated in conditions to be forced to lower case when using the `NC` flag. (markt)

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 2859: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Refactor the code that implements the requirement that a call to `complete()` or `dispatch()` made from a non-container thread before the container initiated thread that called `startAsync()` completes must be delayed until the container initiated thread has completed. Rather than implementing this by blocking the non-container thread, extend the internal state machine to track this. This removes the possibility that blocking the non-container thread could trigger a deadlock. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2860: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fail earlier if the client closes the connection during SNI processing. (markt)

*   ![Image 2862: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[60174](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=60174): Log instances of `HeadersTooLargeException` during request processing. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2863: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[60173](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=60173): Allow up to 64kB HTTP/2 header table size limit. (remm)

### 2016-09-05 Tomcat 9.0.0.M10 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 2876: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[59813](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59813): Ensure that circular relations of the Class-Path attribute from JAR manifests will be processed correctly. (violetagg) 
*   ![Image 2877: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that reading the `singleThreadModel` attribute of a `StandardWrapper` via JMX does not trigger initialisation of the associated servlet. With some frameworks this can trigger an unexpected initialisation thread and if initialisation is not thread-safe the initialisation can then fail. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2878: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Compatibility with rewrite from httpd for non existing headers. (jfclere) 
*   ![Image 2879: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) By default, treat paths used to obtain a request dispatcher as encoded. This behaviour can be changed per web application via the `dispatchersUseEncodedPaths` attribute of the Context. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2880: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Provide a mechanism that enables the container to check if a component (typically a web application) has been granted a given permission when running under a SecurityManager without the current execution stack having to have passed through the component. Use this new mechanism to extend SecurityManager protection to the system property replacement feature of the digester. (markt)

### 2016-07-12 Tomcat 9.0.0.M9 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 2945: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[18500](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=18500): Add limited support for wildcard host names and host aliases. Names of the form `*.domainname` are now permitted. Note that an exact host name match takes precedence over a wild card host name match. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2946: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[57705](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=57705): Add debug logging for requests denied by the remote host and remote address valves and filters. Based on a patch by Graham Leggett. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2947: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct a regression in the fix for [58588](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58588) that removed the entire `org.apache.juli` package from the embedded JARs rendering them unusable. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2948: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[59399](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59399): Add a new option to the Realm implementations that ship with Tomcat that allows the HTTP status code used for HTTP -> HTTPS redirects to be controlled per Realm. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2949: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[59708](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59708): Modify the LockOutRealm logic. Valid authentication attempts during the lock out period will no longer reset the lock out timer to zero. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2950: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Change the default of the `sessionCookiePathUsesTrailingSlash` attribute of the `Context` element to `false` since the problems caused when a Servlet is mapped to `/*` are more significant than the security risk of not enabling this option by default. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2951: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Follow-up to [59655](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59655). Improve the documentation for configuring permitted cookie names. Patch provided by Kyohei Nakamura. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2952: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Do not attempt to start web resources during a web application's initialisation phase since the web application is not fully configured at that point and the web resources may not be correctly configured. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2953: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve error handling around user code prior to calling `InstanceManager.destroy()` to ensure that the method is executed. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 2954: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a cause of multiple attempts to close the same socket. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2955: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor the certificate keystore and trust store generation to make it easier for embedded users to inject their own key stores. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2956: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Add a `maxConcurrentStreamExecution` on the HTTP/2 protocol handler to allow restricting the amount of concurrent stream that are being executed in a single connection. The default is to not limit it. (remm) 
*   ![Image 2957: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[59233](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59233): Add the ability to add TLS virtual hosts dynamically. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2958: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct a problem with `ServletRequest.getServerPort()` for secure HTTP/2 connections that meant an incorrect value was returned when using the default port. (markt)

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 2962: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Now the WebSocket implementation is not built directly on top of the Servlet API and can use Tomcat internals, there is no need for the dedicated WebSocket Executor. It has been replaced by the use of the Connector/Endpoint provided Executor. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2963: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve error handling around user code prior to calling `InstanceManager.destroy()` to ensure that the method is executed. (markt) 

#### Web Applications

*   ![Image 2964: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Do not log an additional case of `IOException`s in the error handler for the Drawboard WebSocket example when the root cause is the client disconnecting since the logs add no value. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2965: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[59642](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59642): Mention the `localDataSource` in the `DataSourceRealm` section of the Realm How-To. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2966: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[59672](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59672): Update the security considerations page of the documentation web application to take account of the fact that the Manager and HostManager applications now have a `RemoteAddrValve` configured by default. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2967: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Follow-up to the fix for [59399](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59399). Ensure that the new attribute `transportGuaranteeRedirectStatus` is documented for all **Realm**s. Also document the `NullRealm` and when it is automatically created for an **Engine**. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2968: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix the description of `maxAge` attribute in jdbc-pool doc. This attribute works both when a connection is returned and when a connection is borrowed. (kfujino) 
*   ![Image 2969: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[59774](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59774): Correct the `prefix` values in the documented examples for configuring the `AccessLogValve`. Patch provided by Mike Noordermeer. (markt)

### 2016-06-13 Tomcat 9.0.0.M8 (markt)

### not released Tomcat 9.0.0.M7 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 2978: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) RMI Target related memory leaks are avoidable which makes them an application bug that needs to be fixed rather than a JRE bug to work around. Therefore, start logging RMI Target related memory leaks on web application stop. Add an option that controls if the check for these leaks is made. Log a warning if running on Java 9 with this check enabled but without the command line option it requires. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2979: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure NPE will not be thrown during deployment when scanning jar files without MANIFEST.MF file. (violetagg) 
*   ![Image 2980: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Remove the `clearReferencesStatic` option from `StandardContext`. It was known to cause problems with some libraries (such as log4j) and was only linked to suspected memory leaks rather than known memory leaks. It had been disabled by default with no increase in the reports of memory leaks for some time. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2981: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[59604](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59604): Correct the assumption made in the URL decoding that the default platform encoding is always compatible with ISO-8859-1. This assumption is not always valid, e.g. on z/OS. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2982: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[59608](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59608): Skip over any invalid `Class-Path` attribute from JAR manifests. Log errors at debug level due to many bad libraries. (remm) 
*   ![Image 2983: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix error message when failed to register MBean. (kfujino) 
*   ![Image 2984: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[59655](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59655): Configure the cookie name validation to use RFC6265 rules by default to align it with the default cookie parser. Document the impact system properties have on cookie name validation. (mark) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 2985: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that requests with HTTP method names that are not tokens (as required by RFC 7231) are rejected with a 400 response. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2986: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When an asynchronous request is processed by the AJP connector, ensure that request processing has fully completed before starting the next request. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2987: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve handling of HTTP/2 stream resets. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2988: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[58750](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58750): The HTTP Server header is no longer set by default. A Server header may be configured by setting the `server` attribute on the `Connector`. A new `Connector` attribute, `serverRemoveAppProvidedValues` may be used to remove any Server header set by a web application. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2989: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[59564](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59564): Correct offset when reading into HTTP/2 input buffer that could cause problems reading request bodies. (violetagg/markt) 
*   ![Image 2990: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Modify the handling of read/write timeouts so that the appropriate error handling (`ReadListener.onError()`, `WriteListener.onError()` or `AsyncListener.onError()`) is called. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2991: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) If an async dispatch results in the completion of request processing, ensure that any remaining request body is swallowed before starting the processing of the next request else the remaining body may be read as the start of the next request leading to a 400 response. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 2992: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[59567](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59567): Fix NPE scanning webapps for TLDs when an exploded JAR has an empty WEB-INF/classes/META-INF folder. (remm) 
*   ![Image 2993: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a memory leak in the expression language implementation that caused the class loader of the first web application to use expressions to be pinned in memory. (markt) 
*   ![Image 2994: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[59654](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59654): Improve error message when attempting to use a TLD file from an invalid location. Patch provided by Huxing Zhang. (markt) 

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 2995: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[59659](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=59659): Fix possible memory leak in WebSocket handling of unexpected client disconnects. (markt) 

#### Web applications

*   ![Image 2996: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58891](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58891): Update the SSL How-To. Based on a suggestion by Alexander Kjäll. (markt) 

#### Extras

*   ![Image 2997: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif)[58588](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58588): Remove the JULI extras package from the distribution. It was only useful for switching Tomcat's internal logging to log4j 1.2.x and that version of log4j is no longer supported. No additional Tomcat code is required if switching Tomcat's internal logging to log via log4j 2.x. (markt) 

#### jdbc-pool

*   ![Image 2998: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a memory leak with the pool cleaner thread that retained a reference to the web application class loader for the first web application to use a connection pool. (markt) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 2999: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Update the internal fork of Commons DBCP 2 to r1743696 (2.1.1 plus additional fixes). (markt)

*   ![Image 3002: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Use UTF-8 with a standard prolog for all XML files. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3003: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58626](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58626): Add support for a new environment variable (`USE_NOHUP`) that causes `nohup` to be used when starting Tomcat. It is disabled by default except on HP-UX where it is enabled by default since it is required when starting Tomcat at boot on HP-UX. (markt)

(markt)

*   ![Image 3093: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Refactor the web.xml parsing so a new parser is created every time the web application starts rather than creating and caching the parser when the Context is created. This enables the parser to take account of modified Context configuration parameters and reduces (slightly) the memory footprint of a running Tomcat instance. (markt)

Components needing access to configuration information may access it via the Servlet API. (markt)

### not released Tomcat 9.0.0.M2 (markt)

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 3149: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor creation of `MapperListener` to ensure that the `Mapper` used is the `Mapper` associated with the `Service` for which the listener was created. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3150: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Move the functionality that provides redirects for context roots and directories where a trailing `/` is added from the Mapper to the `DefaultServlet`. This enables such requests to be processed by any configured Valves and Filters before the redirect is made. This behaviour is configurable via the `mapperContextRootRedirectEnabled` and `mapperDirectoryRedirectEnabled` attributes of the Context which may be used to restore the previous behaviour. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3151: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor `Service.getContainer()` to return an `Engine` rather than a `Container`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3152: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[34319](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=34319): Only load those keys in `StoreBase.processExpire` from JDBCStore, that are old enough, to be expired. Based on a patch by Tom Anderson. (fschumacher) 
*   ![Image 3153: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[56917](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=56917): As per RFC7231 (HTTP/1.1), allow HTTP/1.1 and later redirects to use relative URIs. This is controlled by a new attribute `useRelativeRedirects` on the **Context** and defaults to `true`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3154: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58629](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58629): Allow an embedded Tomcat instance to start when the `Service` has no `Engine` configured. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3155: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correctly notify the MapperListener associated with a Service if the Engine for that Service is changed. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3156: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Make a web application's CredentialHandler available through a context attribute. This allows a web application to use the same algorithm for validating or generating new stored credentials from cleartext ones. (schultz) 
*   ![Image 3157: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58635](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58635): Enable break points to be set within agent code when running Tomcat with a Java agent. Based on a patch by Huxing Zhang. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3158: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fixed potential NPE in `HostConfig` while deploying an application. Issue reported by coverity scan. (violetagg) 
*   ![Image 3159: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58655](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58655): Fix an `IllegalStateException` when calling `HttpServletResponse.sendRedirect()` with the `RemoteIpFilter`. This was caused by trying to correctly generate the absolute URI for the redirect. With the fix for [56917](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=56917), redirects may now be relative making the `sendRedirect()` implementation for the `RemoteIpFilter` much simpler. This also addresses issues where the redirect may not have behaved as expected when redirecting from http to https to from https to http. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3160: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58657](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58657): Exceptions in a Servlet 3.1 `ReadListener` or `WriteListener` do not need to be immediately fatal to the connection. Allow an error response to be written. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3161: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct implementation of `validateClientProvidedNewSessionId` so client provided session IDs may be rejected if validation is enabled. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3162: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58701](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58701): Reset the `instanceInitialized` field in `StandardWrapper` when unloading a Servlet so that a new instance may be correctly initialized. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3163: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Add a new flag `aprPreferred` to the Apr listener. if set to `false`, when using the connector defaults, it will use NIO + OpenSSL if tomcat-native is available, rather than the APR connector. (remm) 
*   ![Image 3164: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add path parameter handling to `HttpServletRequest.getContextPath()`. This is a follow-up to the fix for [57215](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=57215). (markt) 
*   ![Image 3165: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58692](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58692): Make `StandardJarScanner` more robust. Log a warning if a class path entry cannot be scanned rather than triggering the failure of the web application. Includes a test case written by Derek Abdine. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3166: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58702](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58702): Ensure an access log entry is generated if the client aborts the connection. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3167: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fixed various issues reported by Findbugs. (violetagg) 
*   ![Image 3168: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58735](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58735): Add support for the `X-XSS-Protection` header to the `HttpHeaderSecurityFilter`. Patch provided by Jacopo Cappellato. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3169: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add the `StatusManagerServlet` to the list of Servlets that can only be loaded by privileged applications. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3170: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Simplify code and fix messages in `org.apache.catalina.core.DefaultInstanceManager` class. (kkolinko) 
*   ![Image 3171: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58751](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58751): Correctly handle the case where an `AsyncListener` dispatches to a Servlet on an asynchronous timeout and the Servlet uses `sendError()` to trigger an error page. Includes a test case based on code provided by Andy Wilkinson.(markt) 
*   ![Image 3172: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that the proper file encoding if specified will be used when a readme file is served by DefaultServlet. (violetagg) 
*   ![Image 3173: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix declaration of `localPort` attribute of Connector MBean: it is read-only. (kkolinko) 
*   ![Image 3174: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58766](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58766): Make skipping non-class files during annotation scanning faster by checking the file name first. Improve debug logging. (kkolinko) 
*   ![Image 3175: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58836](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58836): Correctly merge query string parameters when processing a forwarded request where the target includes a query string that contains a parameter with no value. (markt/kkolinko) 
*   ![Image 3176: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Make sure that shared Digester is reset in an unlikely error case in `HostConfig.deployWAR()`. (kkolinko) 
*   ![Image 3177: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Extend the feature available in the cluster session manager implementations that enables session attribute replication to be filtered based on attribute name to all session manager implementations. Note that configuration attribute name has changed from `sessionAttributeFilter` to `sessionAttributeNameFilter`. Apply the filter on load as well as unload to ensure that configuration changes made while the web application is stopped are applied to any persisted data. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3178: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Extend the session attribute filtering options to include filtering based on the implementation class of the value and optional `WARN` level logging if an attribute is filtered. These options are available for all of the Manager implementations that ship with Tomcat. When a `SecurityManager` is used filtering will be enabled by default. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3179: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Remove `distributable` and `maxInactiveInterval` from the `Manager` interface because the attributes are never used. The equivalent attributes from the `Context` always take precedence. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3180: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58867](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58867): Improve checking on Host start for WAR files that have been modified while Tomcat has stopped and re-expand them if `unpackWARs` is `true`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3181: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58900](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58900): Correctly undeploy symlinked resources and prevent an infinite cycle of deploy / undeploy. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 3182: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58621](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58621): The certificate chain cannot be set using the main certificate attribute, so restore the certificate chain property. (remm) 
*   ![Image 3183: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Allow a new SSL config type where a connector can use either JSSE or OpenSSL. Both could be allowed, but it would likely create support issues. This type is used by the OpenSSL implementation for NIOx. (remm) 
*   ![Image 3184: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Improve upgrade context classloader handling by using Context.bind and unbind. (remm) 
*   ![Image 3185: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Improve OpenSSL keystore/truststore configuration by using the code from the JSSE implementation. (remm, jfclere) 
*   ![Image 3186: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix a potential loop when a client drops the connection unexpectedly. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3187: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) OpenSSL renegotiation support for client certificate authentication. (remm) 
*   ![Image 3188: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix NIO connector renegotiation. (remm) 
*   ![Image 3189: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58659](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58659): Fix a potential deadlock during HTTP/2 processing when the connection window size is limited. (markt) 

#### Jasper

*   ![Image 3190: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[57136#c25](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=57136#c25): Change default value of `quoteAttributeEL` setting in Jasper to be `true` for better compatibility with other implementations and older versions of Tomcat. Add command line option `-no-quoteAttributeEL` in JspC. (kkolinko) 
*   ![Image 3191: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix handling of missing messages in `org.apache.el.util.MessageFactory`. (violetagg) 

#### Cluster

*   ![Image 3192: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Enable an explicit configuration of local member in the static cluster membership. (kfujino) 
*   ![Image 3193: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix potential integer overflow in `DeltaSession`. Reported by coverity scan. (fschumacher) 
*   ![Image 3194: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) In order to avoid that the heartbeat thread and the background thread to run `Channel.heartbeat` simultaneously, if `heartbeatBackgroundEnabled` of `SimpleTcpCluster` set to `true`, ensure that the heartbeat thread does not start. (kfujino) 

#### WebSocket

*   ![Image 3195: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[55006](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=55006): The WebSocket client now honors the `java.net.java.net.ProxySelector` configuration (using the HTTP type) when establishing WebSocket connections to servers. Based on a patch by Niki Dokovski. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3196: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58624](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58624): Correct a potential deadlock if the WebSocket connection is closed when a message write is in progress. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3197: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[57489](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=57489): Ensure `onClose()` is called when a WebSocket connection is closed even if the sending of the close message fails. Includes test cases by Barry Coughlan. (markt) 

#### Web Applications

*   ![Image 3198: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58631](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58631): Correct the continuation character use in the Windows Service How-To page of the documentation web application. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3199: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct the SSL documentation for deprecated attributes to point to the correct, new location for attributes related to individual certificates. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3200: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct some typos in the JNDI resources How-To. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3201: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Don't create session unnecessarily in the Manager application. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3202: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Don't create session unnecessarily in the Host Manager application. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3203: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif)[58723](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=58723): Clarify documentation and error messages for the text interface of the manager to make clear that version must be used with path when referencing contexts deployed using parallel deployment. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3204: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Document `test.threads` option in BUILDING.txt. (kkolinko) 

#### Tribes

*   ![Image 3205: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Ensure that the static member is registered to the add suspect list even if the static member that is registered to the remove suspect list has disappeared. (kfujino) 
*   ![Image 3206: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) When using a static cluster, add the members that have been cached in the membership service to the map members list in order to ensure that the map member is a static member. (kfujino) 
*   ![Image 3207: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add support for the startup notification of local members in the static cluster. (kfujino)

*   ![Image 3209: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Add support for the shutdown notification of local members in the static cluster. (kfujino) 

#### jdbc-pool

*   ![Image 3210: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Correct evaluation of system property `org.apache.tomcat.jdbc.pool.onlyAttemptCurrentClassLoader`. It was basically ignored before. Reported by coverity scan. (fschumacher) 
*   ![Image 3211: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Fix potential integer overflow in `ConnectionPool` and `PooledConnection`. Reported by coverity scan. (fschumacher)

### 2015-11-17 Tomcat 9.0.0.M1 (markt)

#### General

*   ![Image 3219: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Make Java 8 the minimum required version to build and run Tomcat 9. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3220: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Remove support for Comet. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3221: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Tighten up the default file permissions for the `.tar.gz` distribution so no files or directories are world readable by default. Configure Tomcat to run with a default umask of `0027` which may be overridden by setting `UMASK` in `setenv.sh`. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3222: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Remove native code (Windows Service Wrapper, APR/native connector) support for Windows Itanium. (markt) 

#### Catalina

*   ![Image 3223: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) The default HTTP cookie parser has been changed to `org.apache.tomcat.util.http.Rfc6265CookieProcessor`. (markt) 

#### Coyote

*   ![Image 3224: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) Remove support for the HTTP BIO and AJP BIO connectors. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3225: Code: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/code.gif) Refactor HTTP upgrade and AJP implementations to reduce duplication. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3226: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for HPACK header encoding and decoding, contributed by Stuart Douglas. (remm) 
*   ![Image 3227: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif)[57108](https://bz.apache.org/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=57108): Add support for Server Name Indication (SNI). There has been significant changes to the SSL configuration in server.xml to support this. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3228: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add SSL engine for JSSE backed by OpenSSL. Includes ALPN support. Based on code contributed by Numa de Montmollin and derived from code developed by Twitter and Netty. (remm) 
*   ![Image 3229: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) RFC 7230 states that clients should ignore reason phrases in HTTP/1.1 response messages. Since the reason phrase is optional, Tomcat no longer sends it. As a result the system property `org.apache.coyote.USE_CUSTOM_STATUS_MSG_IN_HEADER` is no longer used and has been removed. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3230: Update: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/update.gif) The minimum required Tomcat Native version has been increased to 1.2.2. The 1.2.x branch includes ALPN and SNI support which are required for HTTP/2. (markt) 
*   ![Image 3231: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Add support for HTTP/2 including server push. (markt) 

#### Tribes

*   ![Image 3232: Fix: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/fix.gif) Clarify the handling of Copy message and Copy nodes. (kfujino) 

#### Other

*   ![Image 3233: Add: ](https://tomcat.apache.org/tomcat-9.0-doc/images/add.gif) Support the use of the `threads` attribute on Ant's junit task. Note that using this with a value of greater than one will disable Cobertura code coverage. (markt)
